  Plus, ZoomIn, ZoomOut, Maximize2, Trash2, Link2,
  Square, Diamond, Circle, Hexagon, X, Settings
} from "lucide-react";

// NodePalette component (v27)
function NodePalette({onAddNode,onClose}){
const [search,setSearch]=useState(””);
const [selCat,setSelCat]=useState(“All”);
const [view,setView]=useState(“grid”);
const filtered=NODE_LIBRARY.flatMap(cat=>
(selCat===“All”||selCat===cat.category)?cat.nodes.filter(n=>!search||n.label.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase())):[]
);
return (
<motion.div initial={{opacity:0,x:320}} animate={{opacity:1,x:0}} exit={{opacity:0,x:320}}
transition={{type:“spring”,stiffness:360,damping:30}}
style={{width:330,flexShrink:0,background:G.glassDeep,backdropFilter:“blur(28px)”,borderLeft:`1px solid ${G.border}`,display:“flex”,flexDirection:“column”,height:“100%”}}>
<div style={{padding:“14px 14px 10px”,borderBottom:`1px solid ${G.border}`,flexShrink:0}}>
<div style={{display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,justifyContent:“space-between”,marginBottom:10}}>
<div style={{display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,gap:7}}>
<div style={{width:26,height:26,borderRadius:9,background:“linear-gradient(135deg,#8b00ff,#ff2d6b)”,display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,justifyContent:“center”}}>
<Layers size={12} color="#fff"/>
</div>
<div>
<p style={{fontFamily:G.fSyne,fontSize:12,fontWeight:800,color:G.pink}}>Node Library</p>
<p style={{fontSize:8,fontFamily:G.fMono,color:G.muted,marginTop:1}}>{filtered.length} nodes</p>
</div>
</div>
<div style={{display:“flex”,gap:4,alignItems:“center”}}>
{[[“grid”,“▦”],[“list”,“≡”]].map(([v,ic])=>(
<button key={v} onClick={()=>setView(v)}
style={{width:24,height:24,borderRadius:7,border:“none”,cursor:“pointer”,background:view===v?`${G.violet}22`:“transparent”,color:view===v?G.violet:G.muted,fontSize:12}}>
{ic}
</button>
))}
<button onClick={onClose} style={{width:24,height:24,borderRadius:7,border:“none”,cursor:“pointer”,background:“rgba(255,45,107,0.12)”,color:G.rose,display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,justifyContent:“center”}}>
<X size={12}/>
</button>
</div>
</div>
<div style={{position:“relative”,marginBottom:8}}>
<Search size={11} color={G.muted} style={{position:“absolute”,left:9,top:“50%”,transform:“translateY(-50%)”}}/>
<input value={search} onChange={e=>setSearch(e.target.value)} placeholder=“Search nodes…”
style={{width:“100%”,background:“rgba(0,0,0,0.4)”,border:`1px solid ${G.border}`,borderRadius:9,padding:“7px 9px 7px 28px”,color:G.text,fontFamily:G.fMono,fontSize:10,outline:“none”,boxSizing:“border-box”}}/>
</div>
<div style={{display:“flex”,gap:3,overflowX:“auto”,paddingBottom:2}}>
{[“All”,…NODE_LIBRARY.map(c=>c.category)].map(cat=>(
<button key={cat} onClick={()=>setSelCat(cat)}
style={{flexShrink:0,padding:“3px 8px”,borderRadius:99,border:“none”,cursor:“pointer”,fontSize:8,fontWeight:800,fontFamily:G.fBody,
background:selCat===cat?“linear-gradient(135deg,#8b00ff,#ff2d6b)”:“rgba(255,255,255,0.06)”,
color:selCat===cat?”#fff”:G.muted}}>
{cat===“All”?“All”:cat.split(” “)[0]}
</button>
))}
</div>
</div>
<div style={{flex:1,overflowY:“auto”,padding:“10px”}}>
{NODE_LIBRARY.filter(cat=>selCat===“All”||selCat===cat.category).map(cat=>{
const catNodes=cat.nodes.filter(n=>!search||n.label.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()));
if(catNodes.length===0)return null;
return (
<div key={cat.category} style={{marginBottom:14}}>
<div style={{display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,gap:6,marginBottom:7,padding:“0 2px”}}>
<div style={{height:1,flex:1,background:`linear-gradient(90deg,${cat.color}40,transparent)`}}/>
<span style={{fontSize:7.5,fontWeight:900,fontFamily:G.fSyne,color:cat.color,textTransform:“uppercase”,letterSpacing:“0.1em”}}>{cat.category}</span>
<div style={{height:1,width:10,background:`${cat.color}40`}}/>
</div>
{view===“grid”?(
<div style={{display:“grid”,gridTemplateColumns:“1fr 1fr 1fr”,gap:5}}>
{catNodes.map(node=>(
<motion.button key={node.type} onClick={()=>onAddNode(node)} whileHover={{scale:1.04,y:-1}}
style={{background:`${node.color}10`,border:`1px solid ${node.color}28`,borderRadius:12,padding:“10px 6px”,cursor:“pointer”,display:“flex”,flexDirection:“column”,alignItems:“center”,gap:5,transition:“border-color 0.15s”}}
onMouseEnter={e=>e.currentTarget.style.borderColor=`${node.color}55`}
onMouseLeave={e=>e.currentTarget.style.borderColor=`${node.color}28`}>
<div style={{width:32,height:32,borderRadius:10,background:`${node.color}18`,border:`1px solid ${node.color}30`,display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,justifyContent:“center”}}>
{React.createElement(node.icon,{size:14,color:node.color})}
</div>
<p style={{fontSize:9,fontWeight:700,fontFamily:G.fBody,color:G.text,textAlign:“center”}}>{node.label}</p>
</motion.button>
))}
</div>
):(
<div style={{display:“flex”,flexDirection:“column”,gap:3}}>
{catNodes.map(node=>(
<motion.button key={node.type} onClick={()=>onAddNode(node)} whileHover={{x:2}}
style={{display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,gap:9,padding:“7px 10px”,background:`${node.color}08`,border:`1px solid ${node.color}22`,borderRadius:9,cursor:“pointer”}}
onMouseEnter={e=>{e.currentTarget.style.background=`${node.color}14`;e.currentTarget.style.borderColor=`${node.color}44`;}}
onMouseLeave={e=>{e.currentTarget.style.background=`${node.color}08`;e.currentTarget.style.borderColor=`${node.color}22`;}}>
{React.createElement(node.icon,{size:13,color:node.color,style:{flexShrink:0}})}
<span style={{fontSize:10,fontWeight:700,fontFamily:G.fBody,color:G.text,flex:1,textAlign:“left”}}>{node.label}</span>
<div style={{width:8,height:8,borderRadius:“50%”,background:node.color,opacity:0.6}}/>
</motion.button>
))}
</div>
)}
</div>
);
})}
{filtered.length===0&&<div style={{textAlign:“center”,padding:“32px 0”,opacity:0.2,color:G.muted,fontSize:11,fontFamily:G.fBody}}>No nodes found</div>}
</div>
<div style={{padding:“8px 14px”,borderTop:`1px solid ${G.border}`,flexShrink:0}}>
<p style={{fontSize:8.5,fontFamily:G.fBody,color:G.dim,textAlign:“center”}}>Click any node to add to canvas</p>
</div>
</motion.div>
);
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  CANVAS ENGINE
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// Canvas Engine (v27) 
function CanvasEngine({state,dispatch}){
const {canvasNodes:nodes,canvasEdges:edges=[],canvasPan:pan,canvasZoom:zoom}=state;
const [selected,setSelected]=useState([]);
const [dragState,setDragState]=useState(null);
const [inspector,setInspector]=useState(null);
const [editLabel,setEditLabel]=useState(null);
const [showPalette,setShowPalette]=useState(false);
const [connectFrom,setConnectFrom]=useState(null);
const containerRef=useRef(null);

const fitView=useCallback(()=>{
if(!nodes.length){dispatch({type:“CANVAS_SET_VIEW”,pan:{x:0,y:0},zoom:1});return;}
const xs=nodes.map(n=>n.x),ys=nodes.map(n=>n.y);
const minX=Math.min(…xs),minY=Math.min(…ys),maxX=Math.max(…nodes.map(n=>n.x+n.w)),maxY=Math.max(…nodes.map(n=>n.y+n.h));
const cw=containerRef.current?.clientWidth||700,ch=containerRef.current?.clientHeight||500;
const scl=Math.min((cw-80)/Math.max(maxX-minX,1),(ch-80)/Math.max(maxY-minY,1),1.5);
dispatch({type:“CANVAS_SET_VIEW”,pan:{x:(cw-((maxX+minX)*scl))/2,y:(ch-((maxY+minY)*scl))/2},zoom:scl});
},[nodes,dispatch]);

const addFromPalette=(nodeType)=>{
const id=`n${Date.now()}`;
dispatch({type:“CANVAS_ADD_NODE”,node:{id,x:100+Math.random()*260,y:60+Math.random()*180,w:155,h:65,
label:nodeType.label,type:nodeType.type,color:nodeType.color,shape:nodeType.shape||“rect”,z:nodes.length+1}});
};

const onCanvasDown=useCallback((e)=>{
if(e.target!==containerRef.current&&!e.target.classList.contains(“cb”))return;
e.preventDefault();
if(connectFrom){setConnectFrom(null);return;}
setSelected([]);setInspector(null);
setDragState({type:“pan”,sx:e.clientX,sy:e.clientY,ox:pan.x,oy:pan.y});
},[pan,connectFrom]);

const onNodeDown=useCallback((e,node)=>{
e.stopPropagation();e.preventDefault();
if(connectFrom&&connectFrom!==node.id){
dispatch({type:“CANVAS_ADD_EDGE”,edge:{id:`e${Date.now()}`,from:connectFrom,to:node.id}});
setConnectFrom(null);return;
}
if(e.shiftKey){setSelected(s=>s.includes(node.id)?s.filter(x=>x!==node.id):[…s,node.id]);}
else{if(!selected.includes(node.id))setSelected([node.id]);setInspector(node.id);}
dispatch({type:“CANVAS_UPDATE_NODE”,id:node.id,patch:{z:nodes.reduce((m,n)=>Math.max(m,n.z||0),0)+1}});
setDragState({type:“node”,sx:e.clientX,sy:e.clientY,ox:node.x,oy:node.y,id:node.id,snapIds:e.shiftKey?selected:[node.id]});
},[selected,nodes,dispatch,connectFrom]);

const onResizeDown=useCallback((e,node)=>{
e.stopPropagation();e.preventDefault();
setDragState({type:“resize”,sx:e.clientX,sy:e.clientY,ow:node.w,oh:node.h,id:node.id});
},[]);

useEffect(()=>{
if(!dragState)return;
const onMove=(e)=>{
const dx=(e.clientX-dragState.sx)/zoom,dy=(e.clientY-dragState.sy)/zoom;
if(dragState.type===“pan”){dispatch({type:“CANVAS_SET_VIEW”,pan:{x:dragState.ox+dx*zoom,y:dragState.oy+dy*zoom},zoom});}
else if(dragState.type===“node”){
const baseNode=nodes.find(x=>x.id===dragState.id);
dragState.snapIds.forEach(id=>{
const n=nodes.find(x=>x.id===id);if(!n||!baseNode)return;
dispatch({type:“CANVAS_UPDATE_NODE”,id,patch:{x:Math.max(0,(id===dragState.id?dragState.ox:n.x)+(dx)),y:Math.max(0,(id===dragState.id?dragState.oy:n.y)+(dy))}});
});
}
else if(dragState.type===“resize”){
dispatch({type:“CANVAS_UPDATE_NODE”,id:dragState.id,patch:{w:Math.max(80,dragState.ow+dx),h:Math.max(44,dragState.oh+dy)}});
}
};
const onUp=()=>setDragState(null);
window.addEventListener(“mousemove”,onMove);window.addEventListener(“mouseup”,onUp);
return()=>{window.removeEventListener(“mousemove”,onMove);window.removeEventListener(“mouseup”,onUp);};
},[dragState,zoom,nodes,dispatch,pan]);

const onWheel=useCallback((e)=>{
e.preventDefault();
const nz=Math.max(0.1,Math.min(4,zoom*(e.deltaY>0?0.92:1.08)));
dispatch({type:“CANVAS_SET_VIEW”,pan,zoom:+nz.toFixed(3)});
},[zoom,pan,dispatch]);

const inspNode=inspector?nodes.find(n=>n.id===inspector):null;

return (
<div style={{display:“flex”,height:“100%”,gap:0}}>
<div style={{flex:1,display:“flex”,flexDirection:“column”,gap:10,overflow:“hidden”}}>
{/* Toolbar */}
<GCard style={{padding:“7px 12px”,borderRadius:14,display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,gap:8,flexWrap:“wrap”,flexShrink:0}}>
<span style={{fontSize:11,fontFamily:G.fSyne,fontWeight:800,color:G.pink,marginRight:4}}>Canvas</span>
<div style={{display:“flex”,gap:4}}>
{[
{icon:ZoomIn,fn:()=>dispatch({type:“CANVAS_SET_VIEW”,pan,zoom:Math.min(4,+(zoom+0.15).toFixed(3))})},
{icon:ZoomOut,fn:()=>dispatch({type:“CANVAS_SET_VIEW”,pan,zoom:Math.max(0.1,+(zoom-0.15).toFixed(3))})},
{icon:Maximize2,fn:fitView},
{icon:RefreshCw,fn:()=>dispatch({type:“CANVAS_SET_VIEW”,pan:{x:0,y:0},zoom:1})},
].map(({icon:Icon,fn},i)=>(
<GBtn key={i} onClick={fn} sm style={{padding:“4px 7px”,borderRadius:8}}><Icon size={11}/></GBtn>
))}
</div>
<span style={{fontSize:9,fontFamily:G.fMono,color:G.muted,padding:“2px 7px”,background:G.glass,borderRadius:6}}>{(zoom*100).toFixed(0)}%</span>
<div style={{width:1,height:16,background:G.border,margin:“0 2px”}}/>
<GBtn onClick={()=>setShowPalette(p=>!p)} sm style={{padding:“4px 10px”,borderRadius:8,background:showPalette?`${G.violet}22`:undefined}}>
<Layers size={11}/>Nodes
</GBtn>
<GBtn onClick={()=>{const id=`n${Date.now()}`;dispatch({type:“CANVAS_ADD_NODE”,node:{id,x:100+Math.random()*250,y:60+Math.random()*180,w:155,h:65,label:“New Node”,type:“process”,color:G.pink,shape:“rect”,z:nodes.length+1}});}} sm>
<Plus size={11}/>Add
</GBtn>
<GBtn onClick={()=>setConnectFrom(connectFrom?null:“select”)} sm style={{background:connectFrom?`${G.violet}22`:undefined}}>
<Link2 size={11}/>{connectFrom?“Cancel”:“Connect”}
</GBtn>
{selected.length>0&&<GBtn onClick={()=>{selected.forEach(id=>dispatch({type:“CANVAS_DELETE_NODE”,id}));setSelected([]);setInspector(null);}} sm>
<Trash2 size={11}/>{selected.length}

Write-File 'src\components\canvas\nodes\CanvasNode.tsx' @'
import { memo } from "react"
import { Handle, Position, NodeProps } from "@xyflow/react"
import { motion } from "framer-motion"
import { Brain, Database, GitMerge, Play, BarChart3, Zap, Box } from "lucide-react"
import { cn, COLORS } from "@/lib/utils"
import type { CanvasNode as CanvasNodeType } from "@/types"

const ICONS: Record<string, React.ReactNode> = {
  process: <GitMerge size={14} />,
  decision: <GitMerge size={14} />,
  data: <Database size={14} />,
  ai: <Brain size={14} />,
  visual: <BarChart3 size={14} />,
  trigger: <Play size={14} />,
  custom: <Box size={14} />,
  manual: <Zap size={14} />
}

const SHAPE_CLASSES: Record<string, string> = {
  rect: "rounded-xl",
  circle: "rounded-full",
  diamond: "", // Handled via CSS clip-path
  hex: "clip-path-hex",
  cloud: "rounded-3xl",
  cylinder: "rounded-lg",
  rounded: "rounded-2xl"
}

function CanvasNode({ data, selected, id }: NodeProps<CanvasNodeType>) {
  const node = data as CanvasNodeType
  if (!node) return null
  
  const isDiamond = node.shape === "diamond"
  const statusColor = node.status ? COLORS.status[node.status] : node.color
  
  return (
    <motion.div
      initial={{ scale: 0.9, opacity: 0 }}
      animate={{ scale: 1, opacity: 1 }}
      whileHover={{ scale: selected ? 1 : 1.02 }}
      className={cn(
        "glass rounded-xl p-3 min-w-[120px] border-2 transition-all cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing focus-ring",
        selected ? "border-violet shadow-lg shadow-violet/20" : "border-white/10 hover:border-white/30",
        SHAPE_CLASSES[node.shape || "rect"],
        isDiamond && "rotate-45"
      )}
      style={{
        background: node.color ? node.color + "15" : undefined,
        borderColor: statusColor ? statusColor + "40" : undefined,
        width: node.width,
        height: node.height
      }}
      tabIndex={0}
      role="button"
      aria-label={node.label}
    >
      {/* Input Handle */}
      <Handle
        type="target"
        position={Position.Left}
        className="w-2.5 h-2.5 bg-violet border-2 border-white shadow-sm"
        aria-label="Input connection point"
      />
      
      {/* Node Content */}
      <div className={cn("flex items-center gap-2 h-full", isDiamond && "-rotate-45")}>
        {/* Icon */}
        <div
          className={cn(
            "w-8 h-8 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center shrink-0",
            node.shape === "circle" && "rounded-full"
          )}
          style={{ background: (node.color || COLORS.violet) + "25" }}
        >
          <span style={{ color: node.color || COLORS.violet }}>
            {ICONS[node.type] || ICONS.process}
          </span>
        </div>
        
        {/* Label & Meta */}
        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
          <p className="text-xs font-bold truncate">{node.label}</p>
          {node.data?.model && (
            <p className="text-[10px] text-white/40 truncate">
              {node.data.model}
            </p>
          )}
          {node.aiGenerated && (
            <span className="inline-block mt-1 text-[9px] bg-violet/20 text-violet px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full">
              AI
            </span>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
      
      {/* Output Handle */}
      <Handle
        type="source"
        position={Position.Right}
        className="w-2.5 h-2.5 bg-emerald border-2 border-white shadow-sm"
        aria-label="Output connection point"
      />
      
      {/* Status Indicator */}
      {node.status && node.status !== "idle" && (
        <span
          className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 w-3 h-3 rounded-full border-2 border-bg"
          style={{ background: statusColor }}
          aria-label={"Status: " + node.status}
        />
      )}
    </motion.div>
  )
}

export default memo(CanvasNode)

// ─── Vault Entry Card (v26) ───────────────────────────────────────
function VaultEntry({ file, onDelete }) {
  const [showLogic, setShowLogic] = useState(false);
  const [showCode, setShowCode] = useState(false);

  return (
    <motion.div 
      layout
      initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
      animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
      className="p-5 rounded-3xl bg-white/[0.02] border border-white/5 hover:border-emerald-500/20 transition-all space-y-4"
    >
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-5">
          <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-2xl bg-emerald-500/10 border border-emerald-500/20 flex items-center justify-center text-emerald-400 shadow-inner">
            <FileCode size={22} />
          </div>
          <div>
            <p className="text-sm font-bold tracking-tight text-white/90">{file.name}</p>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-1.5">
              <Chip color={T.emerald}>{file.ext}</Chip>
              <span className="text-[9px] font-mono text-white/20 uppercase tracking-widest">{Math.round(file.size/1024)} KB</span>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          <button 
            onClick={() => setShowCode(!showCode)}
            className={`p-2.5 rounded-xl transition-all ${showCode ? "bg-amber-500/20 text-amber-500" : "bg-white/5 text-white/40 hover:text-white"}`}
          >
            <Code2 size={16} />
          </button>
          <button 
            onClick={() => onDelete(file.id)} 
            className="p-2.5 rounded-xl bg-white/5 hover:bg-rose-500/20 text-rose-500/40 hover:text-rose-500 transition-all"
          >
            <Trash2 size={16} />
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Logic Abilities Display */}
      <div className="bg-black/20 rounded-2xl border border-white/5 p-4 space-y-3">
        <div 
          className="flex items-center justify-between cursor-pointer" 
          onClick={() => setShowLogic(!showLogic)}
        >
          <p className="text-[9px] font-black text-white/30 tracking-widest uppercase flex items-center gap-2">
            <Activity size={10} /> Logic DNS Abilities
          </p>
          {showLogic ? <ChevronUp size={12} className="text-white/20"/> : <ChevronDown size={12} className="text-white/20"/>}
        </div>
        
        <p className="text-[11px] text-emerald-400/80 italic font-medium leading-relaxed">
          "{file.analysis.corePurpose}"
        </p>

        <AnimatePresence>
          {showLogic && (
            <motion.div 
              initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }} 
              animate={{ height: "auto", opacity: 1 }} 
              exit={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
              className="overflow-hidden space-y-2 pt-2"
            >
              {file.analysis.abilities.map((ability, idx) => {
                const [label, desc] = ability.split(":");
                return (
                  <div key={idx} className="p-3 rounded-xl bg-white/[0.03] border border-white/5 hover:bg-white/[0.05] transition-colors group">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1">
                      <Zap size={10} className="text-violet-500 group-hover:scale-125 transition-transform"/>
                      <span className="text-[10px] font-black text-violet-400 uppercase tracking-tighter">{label.trim()}</span>
                    </div>
                    <p className="text-[10px] text-white/50 leading-relaxed pl-4 border-l border-white/10">
                      {desc ? desc.trim() : "Ability logic extracted from source code pattern."}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                );
              })}
            </motion.div>
          )}
        </AnimatePresence>
      </div>

      {/* Raw Content Preview */}
      <AnimatePresence>
        {showCode && (
          <motion.div 
            initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }} 
            animate={{ height: "auto", opacity: 1 }} 
            exit={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
            className="overflow-hidden"
          >
            <div className="bg-[#02020a] rounded-2xl border border-white/10 p-4 mt-2">
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
                <span className="text-[8px] font-mono text-amber-500/50 uppercase tracking-widest">Raw Source DNA</span>
                <span className="text-[8px] font-mono text-white/20 uppercase">{file.name}</span>
              </div>
              <pre className="text-[10px] font-mono text-white/40 leading-relaxed overflow-x-auto custom-scroll max-h-[200px] whitespace-pre-wrap">
                {file.content || (file.dataUrl ? "[Multimodal Data: Visual DNA indexed]" : "[Binary Stream Encrypted]")}
              </pre>
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>
    </motion.div>
  );
}

// ─── Terminal View (v26) ──────────────────────────────────────────
function TerminalView({ vault, historyCount }) {
  const [lines, setLines] = useState([
    { text: "WHISPERX ZENITH OMEGA OS v26.0", type: "sys" },
    { text: "QUANTUM ENCRYPTION: ACTIVE", type: "sys" },
    { text: "Type 'help' to see available commands.", type: "dim" }
  ]);
  const [input, setInput] = useState("");
  const scrollRef = useRef(null);

  useEffect(() => { scrollRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth" }); }, [lines]);

  const handleCommand = (e) => {
    if (e.key !== 'Enter') return;
    const cmd = input.trim().toLowerCase();
    if (!cmd) return;

    setLines(prev => [...prev, { text: `zenith@omega:~$ ${input}`, type: "input" }]);
    
    let res = "";
    if (cmd === 'help') res = "Available: help, status, ls, clear, version, stats, vault";
    else if (cmd === 'status') res = `Nodes: ONLINE | Assets: ${vault.length} | Latency: 12ms | Encryption: AES-X`;
    else if (cmd === 'ls' || cmd === 'vault') res = vault.length ? vault.map(f => `[${f.ext}] ${f.name} - ${f.analysis.corePurpose}`).join("\n") : "Vault is empty. Upload logic DNA first.";
    else if (cmd === 'version') res = `WhisperX Zenith ${V} (Standard Build 2026-04)`;
    else if (cmd === 'stats') res = `Evolutions: ${historyCount} | Successful Fusions: ${historyCount} | Uptime: 100%`;
    else if (cmd === 'clear') { setLines([]); setInput(""); return; }
    else res = `zenith: command not found: ${cmd}`;

    setLines(prev => [...prev, { text: res, type: "out" }]);
    setInput("");
  };

  return (
    <div className="bg-[#020207] rounded-3xl border border-white/5 h-[460px] flex flex-col overflow-hidden font-mono text-[11px] shadow-2xl">
      <div className="px-4 py-3 bg-white/5 border-b border-white/5 flex items-center justify-between">
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          <div className="w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full bg-rose-500/30" />
          <div className="w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full bg-amber-500/30" />
          <div className="w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full bg-emerald-500/30" />
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-white/20 text-[9px] tracking-widest uppercase">
          <TerminalSquare size={10} /> Zenith_Terminal_Core
        </div>
      </div>
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-5 space-y-1.5 custom-scroll">
        {lines.map((l, i) => (
          <div key={i} className={`whitespace-pre-wrap ${l.type === "sys" ? "text-violet-400 font-bold" : l.type === "input" ? "text-rose-400" : l.type === "dim" ? "text-white/20" : "text-white/70"}`}>
            {l.text}
          </div>
        ))}
        <div className="flex gap-2 items-center">
          <span className="text-emerald-500 font-bold">zenith@omega:~$</span>
          <input value={input} onChange={e => setInput(e.target.value)} onKeyDown={handleCommand}
                 className="bg-transparent border-none outline-none flex-1 text-white caret-rose-500" autoFocus />
        </div>
        <div ref={scrollRef} />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

export const T = {

  violet: '#7000ff',

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// GLASS CARD COMPONENT
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

interface GlassCardProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  className?: string;
  onClick?: () => void;
  hover?: boolean;
  accent?: 'rose' | 'violet' | 'cyan' | 'emerald' | 'amber' | 'blue';
}

export const GlassCard: React.FC<GlassCardProps> = ({
  children,
  className = '',
  onClick,
  hover = true,
  accent = 'rose',
}) => {
  const accentColor = {
    rose: T.rose,
    violet: T.violet,
    cyan: T.cyan,
    emerald: T.emerald,
    amber: T.amber,
    blue: T.blue,
  }[accent];

  return (
    <motion.div
      whileHover={hover ? { y: -8, scale: 1.01, transition: { duration: 0.4 } } : {}}
      onClick={onClick}
      className={`relative group bg-white/[0.01] border border-white/[0.08] backdrop-blur-3xl rounded-[2.5rem] overflow-hidden ${className} transition-all duration-700 
      ${hover ? 'hover:border-white/[0.2] hover:bg-white/[0.04] hover:shadow-[0_60px_120px_rgba(0,0,0,0.95)] cursor-pointer' : ''}`}
    >
      {/* HUD Visual Accents */}
      <div
        className="absolute top-0 left-0 w-20 h-20 border-t-[3px] border-l-[3px] border-transparent group-hover:border-opacity-40 transition-all duration-700 pointer-events-none rounded-tl-[2.5rem]"
        style={{ borderTopColor: hover ? `${accentColor}66` : 'transparent', borderLeftColor: hover ? `${accentColor}66` : 'transparent' }}
      />
      <div
        className="absolute bottom-0 right-0 w-20 h-20 border-b-[3px] border-r-[3px] border-transparent group-hover:border-opacity-40 transition-all duration-700 pointer-events-none rounded-br-[2.5rem]"
        style={{ borderBottomColor: hover ? `${accentColor}66` : 'transparent', borderRightColor: hover ? `${accentColor}66` : 'transparent' }}
      />

      {/* Micro-Readout HUD */}
      <div className="absolute top-6 right-8 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-700 flex flex-col items-end gap-1">
        <span className="text-[7px] font-mono text-white/30 uppercase tracking-[0.5em]">Frame_Lock_Active</span>
        <div className="flex gap-1">
          {[1, 2, 3].map((i) => (
            <div key={i} className="w-1 h-1 rounded-full bg-white/20" />
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>

      {children}
    </motion.div>
  );
};

// LOADING SPINNER

interface LoadingSpinnerProps {
  size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';
  color?: string;
}

export const LoadingSpinner: React.FC<LoadingSpinnerProps> = ({
  size = 'md',
  color = T.rose,
}) => {
  const sizeMap = {
    sm: 'w-8 h-8',
    md: 'w-12 h-12',
    lg: 'w-16 h-16',
  };

  return (
    <motion.div
      animate={{ rotate: 360 }}
      transition={{ duration: 2, repeat: Infinity, ease: 'linear' }}
      className={`${sizeMap[size]} border-4 border-white/10 border-t-white rounded-full`}
      style={{ borderTopColor: color }}
    />
  );
};

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// TOAST NOTIFICATION
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

interface ToastProps {
  message: string;
  type?: 'success' | 'error' | 'info' | 'warning';
}

export const Toast: React.FC<ToastProps> = ({ message, type = 'info' }) => {
  const colorMap = {
    success: T.emerald,
    error: T.rose,
    info: T.cyan,
    warning: T.amber,
  };

  return (
    <motion.div
      initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
      animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
      exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -20 }}
      className="fixed bottom-8 right-8 px-6 py-4 rounded-[2rem] bg-white/[0.05] border border-white/[0.15] backdrop-blur-3xl"
      style={{ borderColor: colorMap[type] }}
    >
      <p className="text-sm font-black uppercase tracking-widest" style={{ color: colorMap[type] }}>
        {message}
      </p>
    </motion.div>
  );
};

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ANIMATED BUTTON
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

interface AnimatedButtonProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  onClick?: () => void;
  disabled?: boolean;
  variant?: 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'ghost';
  icon?: LucideIcon;
  className?: string;
  size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';
}

export const AnimatedButton: React.FC<AnimatedButtonProps> = ({
  children,
  onClick,
  disabled = false,
  variant = 'primary',
  icon: Icon,
  className = '',
  size = 'md',
}) => {
  const variantStyles = {
    primary: 'bg-gradient-to-r from-rose-600 via-violet-800 to-cyan-600 text-white hover:shadow-[0_0_100px_rgba(112,0,255,0.6)]',
    secondary: 'bg-violet-600 text-white hover:shadow-[0_0_100px_rgba(112,0,255,0.6)]',
    ghost: 'bg-white/[0.05] border border-white/[0.2] text-white hover:bg-white/[0.15]',
  };

  const sizeStyles = {
    sm: 'px-6 py-3 text-sm',
    md: 'px-12 py-6 text-base',
    lg: 'px-20 py-12 text-lg',
  };

  return (
    <motion.button
      onClick={onClick}
      disabled={disabled}
      whileHover={!disabled ? { scale: 1.02 } : {}}
      whileTap={!disabled ? { scale: 0.98 } : {}}
      className={`
        rounded-[2rem] font-black tracking-[1em] uppercase transition-all flex items-center justify-center gap-3
        ${variantStyles[variant]} ${sizeStyles[size]} ${className}
        ${disabled ? 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed' : 'cursor-pointer'}
      `}
    >
      {Icon && <Icon size={24} />}
      {children}
    </motion.button>
  );
};

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// STAT DISPLAY
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

interface StatDisplayProps {

  value: string | number;
  color?: string;
  icon?: LucideIcon;
}

export const StatDisplay: React.FC<StatDisplayProps> = ({
  label,
  value,
  color = T.cyan,
  icon: Icon,
}) => (
  <div className="flex flex-col gap-3">
    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
      {Icon && <Icon size={16} style={{ color }} />}
      <span className="text-[12px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.8em] text-white/50">{label}</span>
    </div>
    <p className="text-3xl font-black" style={{ color }}>
      {value}
    </p>
  </div>
);

"use client"
import { useEffect } from "react"
import Sidebar from "@/components/layout/Sidebar"
import Topbar from "@/components/layout/Topbar"
import { useAppStore } from "@/store"
import { Toaster } from "sonner"

export default function AppShell({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  const { theme, settings, notifications, removeNotification } = useAppStore()
  
  // Sync theme to document
  useEffect(() => {
    const t = theme === "system"
      ? window.matchMedia("(prefers-color-scheme: dark)").matches ? "dark" : "light"
      : theme
    document.documentElement.setAttribute("data-theme", t)
  }, [theme])
  
  return (
    <div className="flex h-screen overflow-hidden ambient-bg relative">
      {/* Ambient Background Blobs */}
      {settings.showPetals && (
        <>
          <div className="ambient-blob w-[600px] h-[600px] bg-violet top-[-15%] right-[-10%]" />
          <div className="ambient-blob w-[500px] h-[500px] bg-rose bottom-[-15%] left-[5%]" />
          <div className="ambient-blob w-[400px] h-[400px] bg-cyan top-[40%] left-[20%]" />
        </>
      )}
      
      {/* Sidebar */}
      <Sidebar />
      
      {/* Main Content */}
      <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col overflow-hidden relative z-10">
        <Topbar />
        <main
          className={cn(
            "flex-1 overflow-auto transition-all duration-300",
            settings.compactMode ? "p-3" : "p-4 md:p-6",
            "container mx-auto px-4"
          )}
          role="main"
        >
          {children}
        </main>
      </div>
      
      {/* Toast Notifications */}
      <Toaster
        position="top-right"
        expand={false}
        richColors
        closeButton
        toastOptions={{
          className: "glass-card",
          style: {
            background: "var(--bg-panel)",
            border: "1px solid var(--border-hi)",
            color: "var(--text)",
            borderRadius: "var(--radius-xl)"
          }
        }}
      />
    </div>
  )
}

        ):(
          <motion.div key="upload" initial={{opacity:0,x:14}} animate={{opacity:1,x:0}} exit={{opacity:0,x:14}}>
            <div onDragOver={e=>{e.preventDefault();setDragging(true);}} onDragLeave={()=>setDragging(false)}
              onDrop={e=>{e.preventDefault();setDragging(false);onFileUpload(e.dataTransfer.files[0]);}}
              onClick={()=>fileRef.current?.click()}
              style={{border:`2px dashed ${dragging?G.pink:G.border}`,borderRadius:16,padding:"32px 24px",textAlign:"center",cursor:"pointer",transition:"all 0.2s",background:dragging?"rgba(255,111,160,0.06)":"transparent"}}>
              <Upload size={32} color={dragging?G.pink:G.muted} style={{margin:"0 auto 12px",display:"block"}}/>
              <p style={{fontSize:12,fontWeight:700,color:dragging?G.pink:G.text,fontFamily:G.fBody}}>
                {dragging?"Drop to Unlock":"Drop any file to unlock"}
              </p>
              <p style={{fontSize:10,color:G.muted,fontFamily:G.fBody,marginTop:4}}>Any file format · Unlocks tier 1 features</p>
              <input ref={fileRef} type="file" style={{display:"none"}} onChange={e=>onFileUpload(e.target.files?.[0])}/>
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>

      <button onClick={()=>{dispatch({type:"SET_AUTH",tier:0,user:null});onClose();}}
        style={{width:"100%",marginTop:14,padding:"9px",background:"none",border:`1px solid ${G.border}`,borderRadius:10,cursor:"pointer",color:G.muted,fontFamily:G.fBody,fontSize:10,fontWeight:600}}>
        Continue as Guest (Public only)
      </button>
    </div>
  </motion.div>
</motion.div>
```

);
}

"use client";
import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from "react";
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion";
import { Search, X, Command } from "lucide-react";
import { G, ACCESS } from "@/store/nexus";

function CommandPalette({state,dispatch,onNav,onClose}){
const [q,setQ]=useState(””);
const ref=useRef(null);
useEffect(()=>{setTimeout(()=>ref.current?.focus(),60);},[]);
const allMods=[…new Set(TAXONOMY.flatMap(f=>f.workflows).flatMap(w=>w.categories).flatMap(c=>c.modules))];
const items=allMods.map(id=>{
const wf=TAXONOMY.flatMap(f=>f.workflows).find(w=>w.categories.some(c=>c.modules.includes(id)));
const feat=TAXONOMY.find(f=>f.workflows.some(w=>w.categories.some(c=>c.modules.includes(id))));
return {id,label:id.charAt(0).toUpperCase()+id.slice(1),icon:wf?.icon||Box,color:wf?.color||G.pink,group:feat?.feature||””,tier:ACCESS[id]||0};
});
const filtered=q?items.filter(x=>x.label.toLowerCase().includes(q.toLowerCase())||x.group.toLowerCase().includes(q.toLowerCase())):items;
const canAccess=(tier)=>tier<=state.authTier;

return (
<motion.div initial={{opacity:0}} animate={{opacity:1}} exit={{opacity:0}}
style={{position:“fixed”,inset:0,zIndex:1000,background:“rgba(2,0,8,0.90)”,backdropFilter:“blur(16px)”,display:“flex”,alignItems:“flex-start”,justifyContent:“center”,paddingTop:“10vh”}}
onClick={e=>e.target===e.currentTarget&&onClose()}>
<motion.div initial={{scale:0.88,y:22}} animate={{scale:1,y:0}} exit={{scale:0.88,y:22}}
transition={{type:“spring”,stiffness:400,damping:30}}
style={{width:“100%”,maxWidth:520,background:G.glassMd,backdropFilter:“blur(28px)”,border:`1px solid ${G.border}`,borderRadius:18,overflow:“hidden”}}>
<div style={{display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,gap:9,padding:“12px 15px”,borderBottom:`1px solid ${G.border}`}}>
<Search size={13} color={G.muted}/>
<input ref={ref} value={q} onChange={e=>setQ(e.target.value)}
placeholder=“Search modules, features…”
style={{flex:1,background:“transparent”,border:“none”,outline:“none”,fontSize:13,fontFamily:G.fBody,color:G.text}}/>
<button onClick={onClose} style={{background:`${G.rose}18`,border:`1px solid ${G.borderRose}`,borderRadius:7,padding:“4px 8px”,cursor:“pointer”,color:G.rose,fontSize:10,fontFamily:G.fMono}}>ESC</button>
</div>
<div style={{maxHeight:360,overflowY:“auto”,padding:“5px”}}>
{filtered.map((c,i)=>{const Icon=c.icon; const locked=!canAccess(c.tier); return(
<button key={i} onClick={()=>{if(!locked){onNav(c.id);onClose();}}}
style={{width:“100%”,display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,gap:10,padding:“9px 11px”,background:“transparent”,border:“none”,cursor:locked?“not-allowed”:“pointer”,borderRadius:10,opacity:locked?0.45:1,textAlign:“left”}}
onMouseEnter={e=>!locked&&(e.currentTarget.style.background=G.glassMd)}
onMouseLeave={e=>e.currentTarget.style.background=“transparent”}>
<div style={{width:30,height:30,borderRadius:10,background:`${c.color}18`,border:`1px solid ${c.color}30`,display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,justifyContent:“center”}}>
{locked?<Lock size={12} color={G.muted}/>:<Icon size={12} color={c.color}/>}
</div>
<div style={{flex:1}}>
<p style={{fontSize:12,fontWeight:700,fontFamily:G.fBody,color:G.text,marginBottom:1}}>{c.label}</p>
<p style={{fontSize:9,fontFamily:G.fBody,color:G.muted}}>{c.group}</p>
</div>
<TierBadge tier={c.tier}/>
{!locked&&<ChevronRight size={10} color={G.dim}/>}
</button>
);})}
</div>
<div style={{padding:“7px 16px”,borderTop:`1px solid ${G.border}`,display:“flex”,gap:16,alignItems:“center”}}>
{[[“↵”,“select”],[“↑↓”,“navigate”],[“⌘K”,“toggle”]].map(([k,d])=>(
<span key={k} style={{fontSize:8.5,fontFamily:G.fMono,color:G.dim,display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,gap:4}}>
<kbd style={{background:G.glass,border:`1px solid ${G.border}`,borderRadius:4,padding:“1px 5px”}}>{k}</kbd>{d}
</span>
))}
<TierBadge tier={state.authTier}/>
</div>
</motion.div>
</motion.div>
);
}

'@

Write-File 'src\components\layout\DashboardLayout.tsx' @'
import { useAuth } from "@/_core/hooks/useAuth";
import { Avatar, AvatarFallback } from "@/components/ui/avatar";
import {
  DropdownMenu,
  DropdownMenuContent,
  DropdownMenuItem,
  DropdownMenuTrigger,
} from "@/components/ui/dropdown-menu";
import {
  Sidebar,
  SidebarContent,
  SidebarFooter,
  SidebarHeader,
  SidebarInset,
  SidebarMenu,
  SidebarMenuButton,
  SidebarMenuItem,
  SidebarProvider,
  SidebarTrigger,
  useSidebar,
} from "@/components/ui/sidebar";
import { getLoginUrl } from "@/const";
import { useIsMobile } from "@/hooks/useMobile";
import { LayoutDashboard, LogOut, PanelLeft, Users } from "lucide-react";
import { CSSProperties, useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";
import { useLocation } from "wouter";
import { DashboardLayoutSkeleton } from './DashboardLayoutSkeleton';
import { Button } from "./ui/button";

const menuItems = [
  { icon: LayoutDashboard, label: "Page 1", path: "/" },
  { icon: Users, label: "Page 2", path: "/some-path" },
];

const SIDEBAR_WIDTH_KEY = "sidebar-width";
const DEFAULT_WIDTH = 280;
const MIN_WIDTH = 200;
const MAX_WIDTH = 480;

export default function DashboardLayout({
  children,
}: {
  children: React.ReactNode;
}) {
  const [sidebarWidth, setSidebarWidth] = useState(() => {
    const saved = localStorage.getItem(SIDEBAR_WIDTH_KEY);
    return saved ? parseInt(saved, 10) : DEFAULT_WIDTH;
  });
  const { loading, user } = useAuth();

  useEffect(() => {
    localStorage.setItem(SIDEBAR_WIDTH_KEY, sidebarWidth.toString());
  }, [sidebarWidth]);

  if (loading) {
    return <DashboardLayoutSkeleton />
  }

  if (!user) {
    return (
      <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen">
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-8 p-8 max-w-md w-full">
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-6">
            <h1 className="text-2xl font-semibold tracking-tight text-center">
              Sign in to continue
            </h1>
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground text-center max-w-sm">
              Access to this dashboard requires authentication. Continue to launch the login flow.
            </p>
          </div>
          <Button
            onClick={() => {
              window.location.href = getLoginUrl();
            }}
            size="lg"
            className="w-full shadow-lg hover:shadow-xl transition-all"
          >
            Sign in
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <SidebarProvider
      style={
        {
          "--sidebar-width": `${sidebarWidth}px`,
        } as CSSProperties
      }
    >
      <DashboardLayoutContent setSidebarWidth={setSidebarWidth}>
        {children}
      </DashboardLayoutContent>
    </SidebarProvider>
  );
}

type DashboardLayoutContentProps = {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  setSidebarWidth: (width: number) => void;
};

function DashboardLayoutContent({
  children,
  setSidebarWidth,
}: DashboardLayoutContentProps) {
  const { user, logout } = useAuth();
  const [location, setLocation] = useLocation();
  const { state, toggleSidebar } = useSidebar();
  const isCollapsed = state === "collapsed";
  const [isResizing, setIsResizing] = useState(false);
  const sidebarRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const activeMenuItem = menuItems.find(item => item.path === location);
  const isMobile = useIsMobile();

  useEffect(() => {
    if (isCollapsed) {
      setIsResizing(false);
    }
  }, [isCollapsed]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (!isResizing) return;

      const sidebarLeft = sidebarRef.current?.getBoundingClientRect().left ?? 0;
      const newWidth = e.clientX - sidebarLeft;
      if (newWidth >= MIN_WIDTH && newWidth <= MAX_WIDTH) {
        setSidebarWidth(newWidth);
      }
    };

    const handleMouseUp = () => {
      setIsResizing(false);
    };

    if (isResizing) {
      document.addEventListener("mousemove", handleMouseMove);
      document.addEventListener("mouseup", handleMouseUp);
      document.body.style.cursor = "col-resize";
      document.body.style.userSelect = "none";
    }

    return () => {
      document.removeEventListener("mousemove", handleMouseMove);
      document.removeEventListener("mouseup", handleMouseUp);
      document.body.style.cursor = "";
      document.body.style.userSelect = "";
    };
  }, [isResizing, setSidebarWidth]);

  return (
    <>
      <div className="relative" ref={sidebarRef}>
        <Sidebar
          collapsible="icon"
          className="border-r-0"
          disableTransition={isResizing}
        >
          <SidebarHeader className="h-16 justify-center">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3 px-2 transition-all w-full">
              <button
                onClick={toggleSidebar}
                className="h-8 w-8 flex items-center justify-center hover:bg-accent rounded-lg transition-colors focus:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-ring shrink-0"
                aria-label="Toggle navigation"
              >
                <PanelLeft className="h-4 w-4 text-muted-foreground" />
              </button>
              {!isCollapsed ? (
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
                  <span className="font-semibold tracking-tight truncate">
                    Navigation
                  </span>
                </div>
              ) : null}
            </div>
          </SidebarHeader>

          <SidebarContent className="gap-0">
            <SidebarMenu className="px-2 py-1">
              {menuItems.map(item => {
                const isActive = location === item.path;
                return (
                  <SidebarMenuItem key={item.path}>
                    <SidebarMenuButton
                      isActive={isActive}
                      onClick={() => setLocation(item.path)}
                      tooltip={item.label}
                      className={`h-10 transition-all font-normal`}
                    >
                      <item.icon
                        className={`h-4 w-4 ${isActive ? "text-primary" : ""}`}
                      />
                      <span>{item.label}</span>
                    </SidebarMenuButton>
                  </SidebarMenuItem>
                );
              })}
            </SidebarMenu>
          </SidebarContent>

          <SidebarFooter className="p-3">
            <DropdownMenu>
              <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
                <button className="flex items-center gap-3 rounded-lg px-1 py-1 hover:bg-accent/50 transition-colors w-full text-left group-data-[collapsible=icon]:justify-center focus:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-ring">
                  <Avatar className="h-9 w-9 border shrink-0">
                    <AvatarFallback className="text-xs font-medium">
                      {user?.name?.charAt(0).toUpperCase()}
                    </AvatarFallback>
                  </Avatar>
                  <div className="flex-1 min-w-0 group-data-[collapsible=icon]:hidden">
                    <p className="text-sm font-medium truncate leading-none">
                      {user?.name || "-"}
                    </p>
                    <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate mt-1.5">
                      {user?.email || "-"}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                </button>
              </DropdownMenuTrigger>
              <DropdownMenuContent align="end" className="w-48">
                <DropdownMenuItem
                  onClick={logout}
                  className="cursor-pointer text-destructive focus:text-destructive"
                >
                  <LogOut className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />
                  <span>Sign out</span>
                </DropdownMenuItem>
              </DropdownMenuContent>
            </DropdownMenu>
          </SidebarFooter>
        </Sidebar>
        <div
          className={`absolute top-0 right-0 w-1 h-full cursor-col-resize hover:bg-primary/20 transition-colors ${isCollapsed ? "hidden" : ""}`}
          onMouseDown={() => {
            if (isCollapsed) return;
            setIsResizing(true);
          }}
          style={{ zIndex: 50 }}
        />
      </div>

      <SidebarInset>
        {isMobile && (
          <div className="flex border-b h-14 items-center justify-between bg-background/95 px-2 backdrop-blur supports-[backdrop-filter]:backdrop-blur sticky top-0 z-40">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <SidebarTrigger className="h-9 w-9 rounded-lg bg-background" />
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                  <span className="tracking-tight text-foreground">
                    {activeMenuItem?.label ?? "Menu"}
                  </span>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
        <main className="flex-1 p-4">{children}</main>
      </SidebarInset>
    </>
  );
}

import React from 'react';
import { motion } from 'framer-motion';
import { Link, useLocation } from 'wouter';
import { useAuth } from ' @/_core/hooks/useAuth';
import {
  Home,
  Database,
  GitMerge,
  Terminal,
  History,
  Map,
  LogOut,
  Menu,
  X,
  BarChart3,
  Workflow as WorkflowIcon,
  Users,
  Zap,
  TrendingUp,
  Upload,
  Store,
  Settings as SettingsIcon,
  BookOpen,
  Download,
} from 'lucide-react';

export default function NavBar() {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = React.useState(false);
  const [location] = useLocation();
  const { logout } = useAuth();

  const navItems = [
    { label: 'Home', path: '/', icon: Home },
    { label: 'Vault', path: '/vault', icon: Database },
    { label: 'Forge', path: '/logic-forge', icon: GitMerge },
    { label: 'Advanced', path: '/advanced-synthesis', icon: Zap },
    { label: 'Workflow', path: '/workflow', icon: WorkflowIcon },
    { label: 'Analytics', path: '/analytics', icon: BarChart3 },
    { label: 'Evolution', path: '/evolution-tracker', icon: TrendingUp },
    { label: 'Export', path: '/export', icon: Download },
    { label: 'Import', path: '/import', icon: Upload },
    { label: 'Marketplace', path: '/marketplace', icon: Store },
    { label: 'Settings', path: '/settings', icon: SettingsIcon },
    { label: 'Docs', path: '/documentation', icon: BookOpen },
    { label: 'Team', path: '/collaboration', icon: Users },
    { label: 'Terminal', path: '/terminal', icon: Terminal },
    { label: 'Genesis', path: '/genesis-history', icon: History },
    { label: 'Topology', path: '/topology', icon: Map },
  ];

  const isActive = (path: string) => location === path;

  return (
    <>
      {/* Desktop Nav */}
      <motion.nav
        initial={{ opacity: 0, y: -20 }}
        animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
        className="fixed top-0 left-0 right-0 z-50 bg-gradient-to-b from-[#010108] via-[#02020c] to-transparent backdrop-blur-3xl border-b border-white/[0.1] px-8 py-4"
      >
        <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto flex items-center justify-between">
          <Link href="/">
            <span className="text-3xl font-black tracking-[1em] uppercase cursor-pointer text-rose-500 hover:text-rose-400 transition-all">
              MERGE
            </span>
          </Link>

          {/* Desktop Menu */}
          <div className="hidden md:flex items-center gap-2">
            {navItems.map((item) => {
              const Icon = item.icon;
              const active = isActive(item.path);
              return (
                <Link key={item.path} href={item.path}>
                  <motion.button
                    whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}
                    whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
                    className={`px-4 py-2 rounded-lg font-bold text-xs uppercase tracking-widest flex items-center gap-2 transition-all ${
                      active
                        ? 'bg-white/[0.15] border border-rose-500/50 text-white shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(255,0,85,0.3)]'
                        : 'bg-white/[0.05] border border-white/[0.1] text-white/60 hover:text-white'
                    }`}
                  >
                    <Icon size={14} />
                    {item.label}
                  </motion.button>
                </Link>
              );
            })}
          </div>

          <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
            <motion.button
              onClick={logout}
              whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}
              className="hidden md:flex px-4 py-2 rounded-lg bg-white/[0.05] border border-white/[0.1] text-white/60 hover:text-rose-400 font-bold text-xs uppercase tracking-widest items-center gap-2 transition-all"
            >
              <LogOut size={14} /> Logout
            </motion.button>

            {/* Mobile Menu Button */}
            <motion.button
              onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)}
              className="md:hidden p-2 rounded-lg bg-white/[0.05] border border-white/[0.1] text-white"
            >
              {isOpen ? <X size={24} /> : <Menu size={24} />}
            </motion.button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </motion.nav>

      {/* Mobile Menu */}
      {isOpen && (
        <motion.div
          initial={{ opacity: 0, y: -10 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
          className="md:hidden fixed top-16 left-0 right-0 z-40 bg-[#010108]/95 backdrop-blur-3xl border-b border-white/[0.1] p-4 space-y-2"
        >
          {navItems.map((item) => {
            const Icon = item.icon;
            const active = isActive(item.path);
            return (
              <Link key={item.path} href={item.path}>
                <motion.button
                  onClick={() => setIsOpen(false)}
                  className={`w-full px-4 py-3 rounded-lg font-bold text-sm uppercase tracking-widest flex items-center gap-2 transition-all ${
                    active
                      ? 'bg-white/[0.15] border border-rose-500/50 text-white'
                      : 'bg-white/[0.05] border border-white/[0.1] text-white/60'
                  }`}
                >
                  <Icon size={16} />
                  {item.label}
                </motion.button>
              </Link>
            );
          })}
          <motion.button
            onClick={() => {
              logout();
              setIsOpen(false);
            }}
            className="w-full px-4 py-3 rounded-lg bg-white/[0.05] border border-white/[0.1] text-white/60 font-bold text-sm uppercase tracking-widest flex items-center gap-2 transition-all"
          >
            <LogOut size={16} /> Logout
          </motion.button>
        </motion.div>
      )}
    </>
  );
}

"use client"
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion"
import {
  LayoutDashboard, Presentation, BarChart3, Users, FileText,
  GitMerge, PenTool, Box, FileCode, ChevronLeft, ChevronRight,
  Sparkles, Settings, Moon, Sun
} from "lucide-react"
import { useAppStore } from "@/store"
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"
import type { NavItem } from "@/types"

const MODULE_NAV: NavItem[] = [
  { id: "dashboard", label: "Task Dashboard", icon: "LayoutDashboard", color: "#7000ff", group: "core" },
  { id: "presentation", label: "Presentation", icon: "Presentation", color: "#ff0055", group: "content" },
  { id: "charts", label: "Charts & Graphs", icon: "BarChart3", color: "#00f5a0", group: "viz" },
  { id: "collaboration", label: "Collaboration", icon: "Users", color: "#ffcc00", group: "content" },
  { id: "proposal", label: "E-Bid Proposal", icon: "FileText", color: "#00d4ff", group: "finance" }
]

const CANVAS_NAV: NavItem[] = [
  { id: "canvas", label: "Canvas Flow", icon: "GitMerge", color: "#7000ff", group: "core" },
  { id: "flow", label: "Workflow", icon: "GitMerge", color: "#00f5a0", group: "core" },
  { id: "mermaid", label: "Mermaid", icon: "FileCode", color: "#ffcc00", group: "build" },
  { id: "whiteboard", label: "Whiteboard", icon: "PenTool", color: "#ff0055", group: "build" },
  { id: "nodes", label: "Node Library", icon: "Box", color: "#00d4ff", group: "build" }
]

const ICON_MAP: Record<string, React.ComponentType<any>> = {
  LayoutDashboard, Presentation, BarChart3, Users, FileText,
  GitMerge, PenTool, Box, FileCode, Sparkles, Settings
}

export default function Sidebar() {
  const {
    appMode, activeModule, canvasMode,
    sidebarOpen, setSidebarOpen,
    setActiveModule, setCanvasMode, setAppMode,
    theme, setTheme
  } = useAppStore()
  
  const nav = appMode === "modules" ? MODULE_NAV : CANVAS_NAV
  const groups = Array.from(new Set(nav.map(n => n.group)))
  
  const Icon = (name: string, size: number, color: string) => {
    const Comp = ICON_MAP[name]
    return Comp ? <Comp size={size} style={{ color }} /> : null
  }
  
  return (
    <motion.aside
      animate={{ width: sidebarOpen ? 240 : 72 }}
      transition={{ type: "spring", stiffness: 300, damping: 30 }}
      className="fixed left-0 top-0 h-screen z-sticky flex flex-col glass-hi border-r border-white/5 overflow-hidden"
      role="navigation"
      aria-label="Main navigation"
    >
      {/* Logo */}
      <div className="h-16 flex items-center px-4 border-b border-white/5 shrink-0">
        <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-br from-rose to-violet flex items-center justify-center shadow-lg shadow-violet/20 shrink-0">
          <Sparkles size={18} className="text-white" />
        </div>
        <AnimatePresence>
          {sidebarOpen && (
            <motion.div
              initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -10 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
              exit={{ opacity: 0, x: -10 }}
              className="ml-3 overflow-hidden"
            >
              <p className="text-sm font-black tracking-tight whitespace-nowrap font-display grad-rose-violet">
                WhisperX
              </p>
              <p className="text-[9px] text-white/30 tracking-[0.2em] uppercase font-mono whitespace-nowrap">
                Ultimate v2.0
              </p>
            </motion.div>
          )}
        </AnimatePresence>
      </div>
      
      {/* Nav Groups */}
      <nav className="flex-1 overflow-auto px-2 py-3 space-y-4" role="menubar">
        {groups.map(group => (
          <div key={group}>
            {sidebarOpen && (
              <h4 className="px-3 py-1 text-[10px] font-semibold text-white/40 uppercase tracking-wider">
                {group}
              </h4>
            )}
            <div className="space-y-1">
              {nav.filter(n => n.group === group).map(item => {
                const active = (appMode === "modules" && activeModule === item.id) ||
                              (appMode === "canvas" && canvasMode === item.id)
                
                return (
                  <motion.button
                    key={item.id}
                    whileHover={{ x: sidebarOpen ? 2 : 0 }}
                    whileTap={{ scale: 0.98 }}
                    onClick={() => {
                      if (appMode === "modules") setActiveModule(item.id as any)
                      else setCanvasMode(item.id as any)
                    }}
                    className={cn(
                      "w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2.5 rounded-xl text-sm transition-all focus-ring",
                      active
                        ? "bg-white/10 border border-white/10 text-white"
                        : "text-white/50 hover:text-white hover:bg-white/5",
                      !sidebarOpen && "justify-center"
                    )}
                    style={{
                      background: active ? item.color + "20" : "transparent",
                      border: active ? "1px solid " + item.color + "40" : "1px solid transparent"
                    }}
                    role="menuitem"
                    aria-current={active ? "page" : undefined}
                  >
                    <span className="relative">
                      {Icon(item.icon, 18, active ? item.color : "currentColor")}
                      {item.id === "ai" && (
                        <span className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 w-2 h-2 bg-rose-500 rounded-full animate-pulse" />
                      )}
                    </span>
                    {sidebarOpen && (
                      <>
                        <span className="flex-1 text-left truncate">{item.label}</span>
                        {active && (
                          <motion.div
                            layoutId="active-indicator"
                            className="w-1 h-6 rounded-full"
                            style={{ background: item.color }}
                          />
                        )}
                      </>
                    )}
                  </motion.button>
                )
              })}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </nav>
      
      {/* Bottom Actions */}
      {sidebarOpen && (
        <div className="p-3 border-t border-white/5 space-y-3 shrink-0">
          {/* Theme Toggle */}
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            <span className="text-xs text-white/40">Theme</span>
            <button
              onClick={() => setTheme(theme === "dark" ? "light" : "dark")}
              className="p-1.5 rounded-lg glass hover:bg-white/10 transition-colors focus-ring"
              aria-label={theme === "dark" ? "Switch to light mode" : "Switch to dark mode"}
            >
              {theme === "dark" ? <Sun size={14} /> : <Moon size={14} />}
            </button>
          </div>
          
          {/* AI Provider */}
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            <span className="text-xs text-white/40">AI</span>
            <select
              value={useAppStore.getState().aiProvider}
              onChange={(e) => useAppStore.getState().setAIProvider(e.target.value as any)}
              className="glass rounded-lg px-2 py-1 text-xs bg-transparent focus-ring"
              aria-label="Select AI provider"
            >
              <option value="gemini">Gemini</option>
            </select>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
      
      {/* Collapse Toggle */}
      <div className="p-2 border-t border-white/5 shrink-0">
        <button
          onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(!sidebarOpen)}
          className="w-full flex items-center justify-center p-2 rounded-xl hover:bg-white/5 transition-colors text-white/40 hover:text-white focus-ring"
          aria-label={sidebarOpen ? "Collapse sidebar" : "Expand sidebar"}
        >
          {sidebarOpen ? <ChevronLeft size={16} /> : <ChevronRight size={16} />}
        </button>
      </div>
    </motion.aside>
  )
}

Write-File 'src\components\layout\Topbar.tsx' @'
"use client"
import { useState } from "react"
import { Key, Eye, EyeOff, Bell, Search, Command } from "lucide-react"
import { useAppStore } from "@/store"
import { setGeminiKey, hasGeminiKey } from "@/lib/gemini/client"
import Button from "@/components/ui/Button"
import Badge from "@/components/ui/Badge"
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const MODULE_LABELS: Record<string, string> = {
  dashboard: "Task Dashboard",
  presentation: "Presentation Engine",
  charts: "Charts & Graphs",
  collaboration: "Collaboration",
  proposal: "E-Bid Proposal",
  canvas: "Canvas Flow",
  flow: "Workflow",
  mermaid: "Mermaid Editor",
  whiteboard: "Whiteboard",
  nodes: "Node Library"
}

export default function Topbar() {
  const { appMode, activeModule, canvasMode, sidebarOpen, theme, setTheme } = useAppStore()
  const [showKeyInput, setShowKeyInput] = useState(false)
  const [keyInput, setKeyInput] = useState("")
  const [keyVisible, setKeyVisible] = useState(false)
  
  const activeLabel = MODULE_LABELS[appMode === "modules" ? activeModule : canvasMode]
  const geminiReady = hasGeminiKey()
  
  const handleSetKey = () => {
    if (keyInput.trim().length > 10) {
      setGeminiKey(keyInput.trim())
      setKeyInput("")
      setShowKeyInput(false)
    }
  }
  
  return (
    <header
      className="h-16 flex items-center justify-between px-6 glass-hi border-b border-white/5 shrink-0"
      style={{ marginLeft: sidebarOpen ? 240 : 72 }}
      role="banner"
    >
      {/* Left: Title & Mode */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
        <h1 className="font-display font-bold text-lg grad-rose-violet">
          {activeLabel}
        </h1>
        <Badge color={appMode === "modules" ? "violet" : "emerald"}>
          {appMode}
        </Badge>
      </div>
      
      {/* Center: Search (desktop) */}
      <div className="hidden md:flex items-center flex-1 max-w-md mx-8">
        <div className="relative w-full">
          <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-white/40" size={14} aria-hidden="true" />
          <input
            type="text"
            placeholder="Search..."
            className="w-full glass pl-9 pr-4 py-1.5 rounded-full text-sm outline-none focus-ring placeholder:text-white/30"
            aria-label="Search"
          />
          <kbd className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-[10px] text-white/40 bg-white/5 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded">
            ⌘K
          </kbd>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      {/* Right: Actions */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
        {/* API Key */}
        {showKeyInput ? (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type={keyVisible ? "text" : "password"}
                value={keyInput}
                onChange={(e) => setKeyInput(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="AIza..."
                onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === "Enter" && handleSetKey()}
                className="glass rounded-xl px-3 py-1.5 text-xs w-48 outline-none focus-ring font-mono"
                aria-label="Gemini API key"
              />
              <button
                onClick={() => setKeyVisible(!keyVisible)}
                className="absolute right-2 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-white/40 hover:text-white/70"
                aria-label={keyVisible ? "Hide key" : "Show key"}
              >
                {keyVisible ? <EyeOff size={12} /> : <Eye size={12} />}
              </button>
            </div>
            <Button variant="violet" size="sm" onClick={handleSetKey}>Save</Button>
            <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={() => setShowKeyInput(false)}>Cancel</Button>
          </div>
        ) : (
          <Button
            variant={geminiReady ? "success" : "ghost"}
            size="sm"
            onClick={() => setShowKeyInput(true)}
            className="focus-ring"
            aria-label={geminiReady ? "Gemini API key set" : "Set Gemini API key"}
          >
            <Key size={13} className={cn(geminiReady ? "text-emerald" : "text-white/40")} />
            {geminiReady ? (
              <Badge color="emerald">Ready</Badge>
            ) : (
              <span className="text-white/40 text-xs">Set Key</span>
            )}
          </Button>
        )}
        
        {/* Theme Toggle */}
        <Button
          variant="ghost"
          size="sm"
          onClick={() => setTheme(theme === "dark" ? "light" : "dark")}
          className="focus-ring"
          aria-label={theme === "dark" ? "Switch to light mode" : "Switch to dark mode"}
        >
          {theme === "dark" ? <Sun size={14} /> : <Moon size={14} />}
        </Button>
        
        {/* Notifications */}
        <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" className="focus-ring" aria-label="Notifications">
          <Bell size={14} />
        </Button>
      </div>
    </header>
  )
}
'@

Write-File 'src\components\modules\AIChatBox.tsx' @'
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Textarea } from "@/components/ui/textarea";
import { ScrollArea } from "@/components/ui/scroll-area";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
import { Loader2, Send, User, Sparkles } from "lucide-react";
import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from "react";
import { Streamdown } from "streamdown";

/**
 * Message type matching server-side LLM Message interface
 */
export type Message = {
  role: "system" | "user" | "assistant";
  content: string;
};

export type AIChatBoxProps = {
  /**
   * Messages array to display in the chat.
   * Should match the format used by invokeLLM on the server.
   */
  messages: Message[];

  /**
   * Callback when user sends a message.
   * Typically you'll call a tRPC mutation here to invoke the LLM.
   */
  onSendMessage: (content: string) => void;

  /**
   * Whether the AI is currently generating a response
   */
  isLoading?: boolean;

  /**
   * Placeholder text for the input field
   */
  placeholder?: string;

  /**
   * Custom className for the container
   */
  className?: string;

  /**
   * Height of the chat box (default: 600px)
   */
  height?: string | number;

  /**
   * Empty state message to display when no messages
   */
  emptyStateMessage?: string;

  /**
   * Suggested prompts to display in empty state
   * Click to send directly
   */
  suggestedPrompts?: string[];
};

/**
 * A ready-to-use AI chat box component that integrates with the LLM system.
 *
 * Features:
 * - Matches server-side Message interface for seamless integration
 * - Markdown rendering with Streamdown
 * - Auto-scrolls to latest message
 * - Loading states
 * - Uses global theme colors from index.css
 *
 * @example
 * ```tsx
 * const ChatPage = () => {
 *   const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>([
 *     { role: "system", content: "You are a helpful assistant." }
 *   ]);
 *
 *   const chatMutation = // trpc.ai.chat.useMutation({
 *     onSuccess: (response) => {
 *       // Assuming your tRPC endpoint returns the AI response as a string
 *       setMessages(prev => [...prev, {
 *         role: "assistant",
 *         content: response
 *       }]);
 *     },
 *     onError: (error) => {
 *       console.error("Chat error:", error);
 *       // Optionally show error message to user
 *     }
 *   });
 *
 *   const handleSend = (content: string) => {
 *     const newMessages = [...messages, { role: "user", content }];
 *     setMessages(newMessages);
 *     chatMutation.mutate({ messages: newMessages });
 *   };
 *
 *   return (
 *     <AIChatBox
 *       messages={messages}
 *       onSendMessage={handleSend}
 *       isLoading={chatMutation.isPending}
 *       suggestedPrompts={[
 *         "Explain quantum computing",
 *         "Write a hello world in Python"
 *       ]}
 *     />
 *   );
 * };
 * ```
 */
export function AIChatBox({
  messages,
  onSendMessage,
  isLoading = false,
  placeholder = "Type your message...",
  className,
  height = "600px",
  emptyStateMessage = "Start a conversation with AI",
  suggestedPrompts,
}: AIChatBoxProps) {
  const [input, setInput] = useState("");
  const scrollAreaRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const inputAreaRef = useRef<HTMLFormElement>(null);
  const textareaRef = useRef<HTMLTextAreaElement>(null);

  // Filter out system messages
  const displayMessages = messages.filter((msg) => msg.role !== "system");

  // Calculate min-height for last assistant message to push user message to top
  const [minHeightForLastMessage, setMinHeightForLastMessage] = useState(0);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (containerRef.current && inputAreaRef.current) {
      const containerHeight = containerRef.current.offsetHeight;
      const inputHeight = inputAreaRef.current.offsetHeight;
      const scrollAreaHeight = containerHeight - inputHeight;

      // Reserve space for:
      // - padding (p-4 = 32px top+bottom)
      // - user message: 40px (item height) + 16px (margin-top from space-y-4) = 56px
      // Note: margin-bottom is not counted because it naturally pushes the assistant message down
      const userMessageReservedHeight = 56;
      const calculatedHeight = scrollAreaHeight - 32 - userMessageReservedHeight;

      setMinHeightForLastMessage(Math.max(0, calculatedHeight));
    }
  }, []);

  // Scroll to bottom helper function with smooth animation
  const scrollToBottom = () => {
    const viewport = scrollAreaRef.current?.querySelector(
      '[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]'
    ) as HTMLDivElement;

    if (viewport) {
      requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        viewport.scrollTo({
          top: viewport.scrollHeight,
          behavior: 'smooth'
        });
      });
    }
  };

  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const trimmedInput = input.trim();
    if (!trimmedInput || isLoading) return;

    onSendMessage(trimmedInput);
    setInput("");

    // Scroll immediately after sending
    scrollToBottom();

    // Keep focus on input
    textareaRef.current?.focus();
  };

  const handleKeyDown = (e: React.KeyboardEvent<HTMLTextAreaElement>) => {
    if (e.key === "Enter" && !e.shiftKey) {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleSubmit(e);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div
      ref={containerRef}
      className={cn(
        "flex flex-col bg-card text-card-foreground rounded-lg border shadow-sm",
        className
      )}
      style={{ height }}
    >
      {/* Messages Area */}
      <div ref={scrollAreaRef} className="flex-1 overflow-hidden">
        {displayMessages.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="flex h-full flex-col p-4">
            <div className="flex flex-1 flex-col items-center justify-center gap-6 text-muted-foreground">
              <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-3">
                <Sparkles className="size-12 opacity-20" />
                <p className="text-sm">{emptyStateMessage}</p>
              </div>

              {suggestedPrompts && suggestedPrompts.length > 0 && (
                <div className="flex max-w-2xl flex-wrap justify-center gap-2">
                  {suggestedPrompts.map((prompt, index) => (
                    <button
                      key={index}
                      onClick={() => onSendMessage(prompt)}
                      disabled={isLoading}
                      className="rounded-lg border border-border bg-card px-4 py-2 text-sm transition-colors hover:bg-accent disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50"
                    >
                      {prompt}
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        ) : (
          <ScrollArea className="h-full">
            <div className="flex flex-col space-y-4 p-4">
              {displayMessages.map((message, index) => {
                // Apply min-height to last message only if NOT loading (when loading, the loading indicator gets it)
                const isLastMessage = index === displayMessages.length - 1;
                const shouldApplyMinHeight =
                  isLastMessage && !isLoading && minHeightForLastMessage > 0;

                return (
                  <div
                    key={index}
                    className={cn(
                      "flex gap-3",
                      message.role === "user"
                        ? "justify-end items-start"
                        : "justify-start items-start"
                    )}
                    style={
                      shouldApplyMinHeight
                        ? { minHeight: `${minHeightForLastMessage}px` }
                        : undefined
                    }
                  >
                    {message.role === "assistant" && (
                      <div className="size-8 shrink-0 mt-1 rounded-full bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center">
                        <Sparkles className="size-4 text-primary" />
                      </div>
                    )}

                    <div
                      className={cn(
                        "max-w-[80%] rounded-lg px-4 py-2.5",
                        message.role === "user"
                          ? "bg-primary text-primary-foreground"
                          : "bg-muted text-foreground"
                      )}
                    >
                      {message.role === "assistant" ? (
                        <div className="prose prose-sm dark:prose-invert max-w-none">
                          <Streamdown>{message.content}</Streamdown>
                        </div>
                      ) : (
                        <p className="whitespace-pre-wrap text-sm">
                          {message.content}
                        </p>
                      )}
                    </div>

                    {message.role === "user" && (
                      <div className="size-8 shrink-0 mt-1 rounded-full bg-secondary flex items-center justify-center">
                        <User className="size-4 text-secondary-foreground" />
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                );
              })}

              {isLoading && (
                <div
                  className="flex items-start gap-3"
                  style={
                    minHeightForLastMessage > 0
                      ? { minHeight: `${minHeightForLastMessage}px` }
                      : undefined
                  }
                >
                  <div className="size-8 shrink-0 mt-1 rounded-full bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center">
                    <Sparkles className="size-4 text-primary" />
                  </div>
                  <div className="rounded-lg bg-muted px-4 py-2.5">
                    <Loader2 className="size-4 animate-spin text-muted-foreground" />
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </ScrollArea>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Input Area */}
      <form
        ref={inputAreaRef}
        onSubmit={handleSubmit}
        className="flex gap-2 p-4 border-t bg-background/50 items-end"
      >
        <Textarea
          ref={textareaRef}
          value={input}
          onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
          onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
          placeholder={placeholder}
          className="flex-1 max-h-32 resize-none min-h-9"
          rows={1}
        />
        <Button
          type="submit"
          size="icon"
          disabled={!input.trim() || isLoading}
          className="shrink-0 h-[38px] w-[38px]"
        >
          {isLoading ? (
            <Loader2 className="size-4 animate-spin" />
          ) : (
            <Send className="size-4" />
          )}
        </Button>
      </form>
    </div>
  );
}

const errs=getErrors(state.vault,s1,s2,ability);
const onEvolve=async()=>{
if(!canEvolve){setShowVal(true);return;}
setBusy(true);setBusyMsg(“ZENITH FUSION…”);
try{
const evo=await aiEvolve(bp,ability,bp.content,mx.name);
const entry={…evo,id:`h${Date.now()}`,bName:bp.name,mName:mx.name,ability,ts:new Date().toISOString()};
dispatch({type:“EVO_ADD”,entry});
toast(“Evolution complete: “+evo.newSystemName);

finally{setBusy(false);setBusyMsg(””);}

return (

            <div style={{flex:1}}>
              <p style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,fontFamily:G.fBody,color:G.text}}>{f.name}</p>
              <p style={{fontSize:9,fontFamily:G.fMono,color:G.muted,marginTop:2}}>{f.analysis?.corePurpose}</p>
            </div>
            <Chip color={f.color}>{f.ext}</Chip>
          </motion.div>
        ))}
      </div>
    }
  </GCard>

  {/* Ability selection */}
  {bp&&mx&&s1!==s2&&(
    <GCard hue="gold" style={{padding:"16px"}}>
      <p style={{fontSize:8,fontWeight:900,color:G.amber,fontFamily:G.fSyne,textTransform:"uppercase",letterSpacing:"0.12em",marginBottom:10}}>Select Ability from Matrix</p>
      <div style={{display:"flex",flexDirection:"column",gap:5}}>
        {(mx.analysis?.abilities||[]).map((ab,i)=>{
          const [label]=ab.split(":");
          return (
            <motion.div key={i} onClick={()=>setAbility(ability===ab?"":ab)} whileHover={{scale:1.01}}
              style={{padding:"9px 12px",borderRadius:10,cursor:"pointer",background:ability===ab?"rgba(255,202,48,0.12)":"rgba(255,255,255,0.03)",border:`1px solid ${ability===ab?G.amber:G.border}`,display:"flex",gap:8,alignItems:"flex-start",transition:"all 0.15s"}}>
              <Zap size={10} color={ability===ab?G.amber:G.dim} style={{flexShrink:0,marginTop:2}}/>
              <p style={{fontSize:10,fontFamily:G.fBody,color:G.text,lineHeight:1.4}}>{ab}</p>
            </motion.div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </GCard>
  )}

  {/* Execute */}
  <GBtn accent onClick={onEvolve} disabled={!canEvolve} style={{padding:"16px",borderRadius:14,justifyContent:"center",fontSize:13}}>
    <Zap size={15}/>EXECUTE EVOLUTION FUSION
  </GBtn>
</div>
```

);
};

// ════ ArchiveView ════
