// AI Terminal View — full interactive

// ════ AITerminalView ════
const AITerminalView=({state,dispatch})=>{
const [input,setInput]=useState(””);
const [history,setHistory]=useState([]);
const [histIdx,setHistIdx]=useState(-1);
const [isTyping,setIsTyping]=useState(false);
const [chatMessages,setChatMessages]=useState([]);
const scrollRef=useRef(null);

useEffect(()=>{ scrollRef.current?.scrollIntoView({behavior:“smooth”}); },[state.terminalLines,isTyping]);

const runCmd=async(cmd)=>{
const line=cmd.trim().toLowerCase();
dispatch({type:“TERMINAL_ADD”,line:{text:`> ${cmd}`,type:“input”}});
setHistory(h=>[cmd,…h.slice(0,49)]);
setHistIdx(-1);
setInput(””);
if(line===“help”){
[“Available commands:”,”  help         — show commands”,”  clear        — clear terminal”,”  vault        — show vault files”,”  history      — show evolution history”,”  status       — system status”,”  version      — version info”,”  ai <message> — chat with AI”].forEach(t=>dispatch({type:“TERMINAL_ADD”,line:{text:t,type:“dim”}}));
} else if(line===“clear”){dispatch({type:“TERMINAL_CLEAR”});}
else if(line===“vault”){
if(state.vault.length===0)dispatch({type:“TERMINAL_ADD”,line:{text:“Vault is empty.”,type:“warn”}});
else state.vault.forEach(f=>dispatch({type:“TERMINAL_ADD”,line:{text:`  [${f.status.toUpperCase()}] ${f.name} (${f.ext} · ${Math.round(f.size/1024)}KB)`,type:“dim”}}));
} else if(line===“history”){
if(state.evoHistory.length===0)dispatch({type:“TERMINAL_ADD”,line:{text:“No evolution history.”,type:“warn”}});
else state.evoHistory.forEach(h=>dispatch({type:“TERMINAL_ADD”,line:{text:`  ${h.newSystemName} [${h.evolutionScore}%] — ${h.bName} → ${h.mName}`,type:“dim”}}));
} else if(line===“status”){
[“SYSTEM STATUS:”,”  Auth Tier:   “+[“Guest”,“File”,“Login”,“Admin”][state.authTier||0],”  Vault Files: “+state.vault.length,”  Evolutions:  “+state.evoHistory.length,”  AI Engine:   CLAUDE SONNET ONLINE”,”  Canvas:      “+state.canvasNodes.length+” nodes”,“STATUS: NOMINAL”].forEach((t,i)=>dispatch({type:“TERMINAL_ADD”,line:{text:t,type:i===6?“sys”:“dim”}}));
} else if(line===“version”){
dispatch({type:“TERMINAL_ADD”,line:{text:`WhisperX NEXUS PRIME ${V}`,type:“sys”}});
} else if(line.startsWith(“ai “)){
const msg=cmd.slice(3).trim();
const newMessages=[…chatMessages,{role:“user”,content:msg}];
setChatMessages(newMessages);
setIsTyping(true);
try{
const response=await aiChat(newMessages);
setChatMessages(m=>[…m,{role:“assistant”,content:response}]);
dispatch({type:“TERMINAL_ADD”,line:{text:response,type:“ai”}});
}catch(e){
dispatch({type:“TERMINAL_ADD”,line:{text:“AI Error: “+e.message,type:“error”}});
}finally{setIsTyping(false);}
} else {
dispatch({type:“TERMINAL_ADD”,line:{text:`Command not found: '${cmd}'. Type 'help'.`,type:“error”}});
}
};

const lineColor=(type)=>{
if(type===“sys”) return G.emerald;
if(type===“input”) return G.pink;
if(type===“ai”) return G.lav;
if(type===“error”) return G.red;
if(type===“warn”) return G.amber;
return G.muted;
};

return (
<div style={{display:“flex”,flexDirection:“column”,height:“100%”,background:”#020208”,borderRadius:16,border:`1px solid ${G.border}`,overflow:“hidden”}}>
{/* Terminal header */}
<div style={{padding:“10px 16px”,background:“rgba(255,255,255,0.04)”,borderBottom:`1px solid ${G.border}`,display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,gap:10,flexShrink:0}}>
<div style={{display:“flex”,gap:5}}>
{[G.red,G.amber,G.emerald].map(c=><div key={c} style={{width:10,height:10,borderRadius:“50%”,background:c}}/>)}
</div>
<span style={{fontFamily:G.fMono,fontSize:10,color:G.muted,flex:1,textAlign:“center”,letterSpacing:“0.15em”}}>NEXUS PRIME TERMINAL v{V}</span>
<StatusDot color={G.emerald} pulse/>
</div>

```
  {/* Output */}
  <div style={{flex:1,overflowY:"auto",padding:"14px 16px",fontFamily:G.fMono,fontSize:10.5}}>
    {state.terminalLines.map((line,i)=>(
      <div key={i} style={{color:lineColor(line.type),lineHeight:1.7,whiteSpace:"pre-wrap",marginBottom:1}}>
        {line.text}
      </div>
    ))}
    {isTyping&&(
      <div style={{color:G.lav,display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:6}}>
        <motion.span animate={{opacity:[0,1,0]}} transition={{repeat:Infinity,duration:0.8}}>█</motion.span>
        <span style={{fontSize:9,opacity:0.6}}>AI thinking…</span>
      </div>
    )}
    <div ref={scrollRef}/>
  </div>

  {/* Input */}
  <div style={{padding:"10px 16px",borderTop:`1px solid ${G.border}`,display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:8,flexShrink:0,background:"rgba(0,0,0,0.3)"}}>
    <span style={{color:G.violet,fontFamily:G.fMono,fontSize:12,flexShrink:0}}>❯</span>
    <input value={input} onChange={e=>setInput(e.target.value)}
      onKeyDown={e=>{
        if(e.key==="Enter"&&input.trim())runCmd(input);
        if(e.key==="ArrowUp"){const idx=Math.min(histIdx+1,history.length-1);setHistIdx(idx);setInput(history[idx]||"");}
        if(e.key==="ArrowDown"){const idx=Math.max(histIdx-1,-1);setHistIdx(idx);setInput(idx===-1?"":history[idx]||"");}
      }}
      placeholder="Type a command or 'ai <message>'…"
      style={{flex:1,background:"transparent",border:"none",outline:"none",color:G.text,fontFamily:G.fMono,fontSize:11}}
      autoFocus/>
  </div>
</div>
```

);
};

</div>
</div>
<div style={{display:“flex”,gap:4,flexDirection:“column”,alignItems:“flex-end”}}>
{c.tag&&<Chip color={c.tag===“admin”?G.rose:c.tag===“system”?G.violet:G.cyan}>{c.tag}</Chip>}
<button onClick={()=>dispatch({type:“CONTACT_DELETE”,id:c.id})} style={{background:“none”,border:“none”,cursor:“pointer”,color:G.rose,display:“flex”,marginTop:4}}>
<Trash2 size={12}/>
</button>
</div>
</div>
</GCard>
))}
</div>
</div>
);
};

// Budget View

// ════ BudgetView ════
const BudgetView=({state,dispatch,toast})=>{
const [adding,setAdding]=useState(false);
const [form,setForm]=useState({label:””,amount:””,type:“expense”,tag:””});
const income=state.budget.filter(b=>b.type===“income”).reduce((s,b)=>s+b.amount,0);
const expense=state.budget.filter(b=>b.type===“expense”).reduce((s,b)=>s+b.amount,0);
return (
<div style={{display:“flex”,flexDirection:“column”,gap:14}}>
<div style={{display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,gap:10}}>
<h1 style={{fontFamily:G.fSyne,fontSize:22,fontWeight:800,color:G.text,flex:1}}>Budget</h1>
<GBtn onClick={()=>setAdding(a=>!a)} sm><Plus size={11}/>Add</GBtn>
</div>
<div style={{display:“grid”,gridTemplateColumns:“repeat(3,1fr)”,gap:10}}>
{[{l:“Revenue”,v:income,c:G.emerald},{l:“Expenses”,v:expense,c:G.rose},{l:“Net”,v:income-expense,c:(income-expense)>=0?G.emerald:G.rose}].map(({l,v,c})=>(
<GCard key={l} style={{padding:“14px”,textAlign:“center”}}>
<p style={{fontSize:9,color:G.muted,fontFamily:G.fBody,marginBottom:6,textTransform:“uppercase”,letterSpacing:“0.1em”}}>{l}</p>
<p style={{fontSize:22,fontWeight:900,fontFamily:G.fSyne,color:c}}>${v.toLocaleString()}</p>
</GCard>
))}
</div>
<AnimatePresence>
{adding&&(
<motion.div initial={{height:0,opacity:0}} animate={{height:“auto”,opacity:1}} exit={{height:0,opacity:0}} style={{overflow:“hidden”}}>
<GCard style={{padding:“14px”,display:“flex”,flexDirection:“column”,gap:10}}>
{[[“label”,“Label”],[“amount”,“Amount”],[“tag”,“Tag”]].map(([k,lbl])=>(
<div key={k}>
<p style={{fontSize:9,fontWeight:900,color:G.muted,fontFamily:G.fBody,textTransform:“uppercase”,letterSpacing:“0.1em”,marginBottom:4}}>{lbl}</p>
<input value={form[k]} onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({…f,[k]:e.target.value}))} type={k===“amount”?“number”:“text”}
style={{width:“100%”,background:“rgba(0,0,0,0.4)”,border:`1px solid ${G.border}`,borderRadius:9,padding:“8px 12px”,color:G.text,fontFamily:G.fBody,fontSize:11,outline:“none”,boxSizing:“border-box”}}/>
</div>
))}
<div style={{display:“flex”,gap:6}}>
{[“expense”,“income”].map(t=>(
<button key={t} onClick={()=>setForm(f=>({…f,type:t}))}
style={{flex:1,padding:“8px”,borderRadius:8,border:“none”,cursor:“pointer”,fontFamily:G.fBody,fontSize:10,fontWeight:700,background:form.type===t?`${t==="income"?G.emerald:G.rose}22`:“rgba(255,255,255,0.05)”,color:form.type===t?t===“income”?G.emerald:G.rose:G.muted}}>
{t}
</button>
))}
</div>
<GBtn accent onClick={()=>{
if(!form.label||!form.amount)return;
dispatch({type:“BUDGET_ADD”,item:{id:`b${Date.now()}`,…form,amount:parseFloat(form.amount)}});
setForm({label:””,amount:””,type:“expense”,tag:””});setAdding(false);toast(“Entry added.”);
}}>Save Entry</GBtn>
</GCard>
</motion.div>
)}
</AnimatePresence>
<div style={{display:“flex”,flexDirection:“column”,gap:7}}>
{state.budget.map(b=>(
<GCard key={b.id} style={{padding:“12px 14px”}}>
<div style={{display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,gap:10}}>
<div style={{width:36,height:36,borderRadius:11,background:`${b.type==="income"?G.emerald:G.rose}14`,border:`1px solid ${b.type==="income"?G.emerald:G.rose}28`,display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,justifyContent:“center”,flexShrink:0}}>
{b.type===“income”?<TrendingUp size={16} color={G.emerald}/>:<DollarSign size={16} color={G.rose}/>}
</div>
<div style={{flex:1}}>
<p style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,fontFamily:G.fBody,color:G.text}}>{b.label}</p>
<p style={{fontSize:9,fontFamily:G.fMono,color:G.muted,marginTop:1}}>{b.date} · {b.tag}</p>
</div>
<p style={{fontSize:15,fontWeight:900,fontFamily:G.fSyne,color:b.type===“income”?G.emerald:G.rose}}>
{b.type===“income”?”+”:”-”}${b.amount.toLocaleString()}
</p>
<button onClick={()=>dispatch({type:“BUDGET_DELETE”,id:b.id})} style={{background:“none”,border:“none”,cursor:“pointer”,color:G.muted,display:“flex”}}>
<Trash2 size={12}/>
</button>
</div>
</GCard>
))}
</div>
</div>
);
};

const colorMap: Record<BadgeColor, string> = {

  violet: "bg-violet/15 text-violet border-violet/25",
  emerald: "bg-emerald/15 text-emerald border-emerald/25",

  cyan: "bg-cyan/15 text-cyan border-cyan/25",
  blue: "bg-blue/15 text-blue border-blue/25",
  gray: "bg-white/10 text-white/50 border-white/10"
}

export default function Badge({
  children,
  color = "violet",
  className
}: {
  children: ReactNode
  color?: BadgeColor

}) {

    )}>
      {children}
    </span>
  )
}

Write-File 'src\components\ui\Button.tsx' @'
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"
import { motion, HTMLMotionProps } from "framer-motion"
import { Loader2 } from "lucide-react"
import type { ButtonProps } from "@/types"

const variants: Record<string, string> = {
  primary: "bg-gradient-to-r from-rose to-violet text-white hover:from-rose/90 hover:to-violet/90 shadow-lg shadow-violet/25 border-0",
  secondary: "bg-white/5 text-white border border-white/20 hover:bg-white/10 hover:border-white/30",
  ghost: "bg-transparent text-white/80 hover:text-white hover:bg-white/5 border border-transparent",
  danger: "bg-rose/10 text-rose border border-rose/30 hover:bg-rose/20 hover:border-rose/50",
  success: "bg-emerald/10 text-emerald border border-emerald/30 hover:bg-emerald/20 hover:border-emerald/50",
  warning: "bg-amber/10 text-amber border border-amber/30 hover:bg-amber/20 hover:border-amber/50",
  glass: "glass text-white/80 hover:text-white hover:bg-white/10"
}

const sizes: Record<string, string> = {
  xs: "px-2.5 py-1 text-[10px] rounded-xl gap-1 h-7",
  sm: "px-3 py-1.5 text-xs rounded-xl gap-1 h-8",
  md: "px-5 py-2.5 text-sm rounded-2xl gap-1.5 h-10",
  lg: "px-7 py-3.5 text-base rounded-3xl gap-2 h-12",
  xl: "px-9 py-4 text-lg rounded-3xl gap-2.5 h-14"
}

export default function Button({
  children,
  variant = "ghost",
  size = "md",
  disabled,
  loading,
  className,
  onClick,
  type = "button",
  icon,
  fullWidth = false,
  pill = true,
  ...props
}: ButtonProps) {
  const shape = pill ? "rounded-full" : sizes[size].includes("rounded-") ? sizes[size].match(/rounded-\w+/)?.[0] || "rounded-xl" : "rounded-xl"
  const width = fullWidth ? "w-full" : ""
  
  return (
    <motion.button
      whileHover={{ scale: disabled ? 1 : 1.02 }}
      whileTap={{ scale: disabled ? 1 : 0.97 }}
      type={type}
      disabled={disabled || loading}
      onClick={onClick}
      className={cn(
        "btn-base focus-ring relative overflow-hidden",
        variants[variant],
        sizes[size].replace(/rounded-\w+/, ""),
        shape,
        width,
        (disabled || loading) && "opacity-40 cursor-not-allowed",
        className
      )}
      {...(props as HTMLMotionProps<"button">)}
    >
      {loading && (
        <span className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center">
          <Loader2 className="animate-spin" size={size === "xs" ? 10 : size === "sm" ? 12 : size === "lg" ? 20 : 16} />
        </span>
      )}
      <span className={cn("flex items-center", loading && "opacity-0")}>
        {!loading && icon && <span className={cn("shrink-0", size === "xs" ? "h-3 w-3" : size === "sm" ? "h-3.5 w-3.5" : size === "lg" ? "h-5 w-5" : "h-4 w-4")}>{icon}</span>}
        {children}
      </span>
      {variant === "primary" && (
        <span className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-white/0 via-white/10 to-white/0 translate-x-[-100%] hover:translate-x-[100%] transition-transform duration-700" />
      )}
    </motion.button>
  )
}

Write-File 'src\components\ui\Card.tsx' @'
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"
import type { CardProps } from "@/types"

export default function Card({
  children,
  className,
  glow = "none",
  padded = true,
  hover = true,
  onClick,
  role,
  ariaLabel
}: CardProps) {
  const glowClass = glow !== "none" ? {
    rose: "shadow-glow-rose hover:shadow-glow-rose/80",
    violet: "shadow-glow-violet hover:shadow-glow-violet/80",
    emerald: "shadow-glow-emerald hover:shadow-glow-emerald/80"
  }[glow] : ""
  
  return (
    <div
      role={role}
      aria-label={ariaLabel}
      onClick={onClick}
      className={cn(
        "glass-card focus-ring",
        padded && "p-5",
        hover && "hover:-translate-y-0.5 transition-all duration-300",
        glowClass,
        className
      )}
    >
      {children}
    </div>
  )
}

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"
import type { InputProps } from "@/types"

export default function Input({
  label,
  error,
  hint,
  icon,
  rightAddon,
  fullWidth = true,
  className,
  ...props
}: InputProps) {
  return (
    <div className={cn("flex flex-col gap-1.5", fullWidth && "w-full")}>
      {label && (
        <label className="text-xs font-bold text-white/40 uppercase tracking-widest">
          {label}
        </label>
      )}
      <div className="relative">
        {icon && (
          <span className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-white/40 pointer-events-none">
            {icon}
          </span>
        )}
        <input
          className={cn(
            "w-full bg-black/40 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl px-4 py-2.5 text-sm text-white placeholder:text-white/20 outline-none transition-all focus-ring",
            "focus:border-violet/50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-violet/10",
            icon && "pl-10",
            rightAddon && "pr-10",
            error && "border-rose/50 focus:border-rose/50 focus:ring-rose/10",
            props.disabled && "opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed",
            className
          )}
          {...props}
        />
        {rightAddon && (
          <span className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2">
            {rightAddon}
          </span>
        )}
      </div>
      {error && <p className="text-xs text-rose">{error}</p>}
      {hint && !error && <p className="text-xs text-white/40">{hint}</p>}
    </div>
  )
}

Write-File 'src\components\ui\Modal.tsx' @'
"use client"
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion"
import { X } from "lucide-react"
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"
import type { ReactNode } from "react"

export default function Modal({
  open,
  onClose,
  title,
  children,
  width = "max-w-2xl",
  closeOnEscape = true,
  closeOnOverlay = true
}: {
  open: boolean
  onClose: () => void
  title?: string
  children: ReactNode
  width?: string
  closeOnEscape?: boolean
  closeOnOverlay?: boolean
}) {
  // Escape key handler
  if (typeof window !== "undefined" && closeOnEscape) {
    // Handler attached in useEffect in real usage
  }
  
  return (
    <AnimatePresence>
      {open && (
        <motion.div
          initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
          exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
          className="fixed inset-0 z-modal flex items-center justify-center p-4 bg-black/70 backdrop-blur-xl"
          onClick={closeOnOverlay ? onClose : undefined}
          role="dialog"
          aria-modal="true"
          aria-labelledby={title ? "modal-title" : undefined}
        >
          <motion.div
            initial={{ scale: 0.95, opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
            animate={{ scale: 1, opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
            exit={{ scale: 0.95, opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
            transition={{ type: "spring", damping: 25, stiffness: 300 }}
            className={cn(
              "glass-hi rounded-3xl p-6 w-full relative z-10 flex flex-col max-h-[90vh]",
              width
            )}
            onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
          >
            {title && (
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-5 pb-4 border-b border-white/10">
                <h3 id="modal-title" className="text-lg font-black font-display">
                  {title}
                </h3>
                <button
                  onClick={onClose}
                  className="p-2 rounded-xl hover:bg-white/10 transition-colors focus-ring"
                  aria-label="Close modal"
                >
                  <X size={18} />
                </button>
              </div>
            )}
            <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto pr-2">
              {children}
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        </motion.div>
      )}
    </AnimatePresence>
  )
}

function NexusField(){

</defs>
<rect width="100%" height="100%" fill="url(#npgrid)"/>
</svg>

<svg style={{position:“absolute”,right:“3%”,bottom:“4%”,opacity:0.022,width:280,height:280}}>

fill=“none” stroke=”#ff2d6b” strokeWidth=“1”
transform={`rotate(${a} 140 140)`}/>)}
<circle cx="140" cy="140" r="18" fill="#8b00ff" opacity="0.5"/>
</svg>
</div>
);
}

style={{position:“fixed”,bottom:70,left:“50%”,transform:“translateX(-50%)”,zIndex:3000,

</motion.div>

}

Write-File 'src\components\vision\VisionImport.tsx' @'
"use client";
import { useState, useRef, useCallback } from "react";
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion";
import { useDropzone } from "react-dropzone";
import {
  Camera, Upload, Image, Cpu, CheckCircle2, XCircle,
  Loader2, Sparkles, Download, Copy, CheckCheck, X
} from "lucide-react";
import { type VisionStageState, PIPELINE_STAGES } from "@/lib/vision/pipeline";

const STAGE_LABELS: Record<string, string> = {
  blueprint: "Blueprint Analysis",
  tokens:    "Design Tokens",
  patterns:  "Pattern Recognition",
  codegen:   "Structure Generation",
  rules:     "Rule Application",
  refine:    "Lockspec Synthesis",
  export:    "Package & Export",
};

const STAGE_COLOR: Record<string, string> = {
  idle:    "rgba(255,255,255,0.1)",
  running: "#ffca30",
  done:    "#00f5a0",
  error:   "#ff0055",
};

export default function VisionImport() {
  const [image, setImage] = useState<{dataUrl:string; base64:string; mime:string; name:string} | null>(null);
  const [stages, setStages] = useState<VisionStageState[]>(PIPELINE_STAGES);
  const [running, setRunning] = useState(false);
  const [result, setResult] = useState<{lockspecText:string; sourceName:string; totalTokens:number} | null>(null);
  const [error, setError] = useState("");
  const [copied, setCopied] = useState(false);

  const { getRootProps, getInputProps, isDragActive } = useDropzone({
    accept: { "image/*": [] },
    maxFiles: 1,
    onDrop: (files) => {
      const file = files[0];
      if (!file) return;
      const reader = new FileReader();
      reader.onload = (e) => {
        const dataUrl = e.target?.result as string;
        setImage({ dataUrl, base64: dataUrl.split(",")[1], mime: file.type, name: file.name });
        setResult(null);
        setError("");
        setStages(PIPELINE_STAGES);
      };
      reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    },
  });

  const runPipeline = async () => {
    if (!image) return;
    setRunning(true);
    setError("");
    setResult(null);
    try {
      const res = await fetch("/api/ai/vision-pipeline", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ imageBase64: image.base64, imageMimeType: image.mime }),
      });
      const data = await res.json() as {
        lockspecText?: string; sourceName?: string; totalTokens?: number;
        stages?: VisionStageState[]; error?: string;
      };
      if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
      if (data.stages) setStages(data.stages);
      setResult({
        lockspecText: data.lockspecText ?? "",
        sourceName: data.sourceName ?? image.name,
        totalTokens: data.totalTokens ?? 0,
      });
    } catch (e: unknown) {
      setError(e instanceof Error ? e.message : "Pipeline failed");
    } finally {
      setRunning(false);
    }
  };

  const copy = () => {
    if (!result) return;
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(result.lockspecText);
    setCopied(true);
    setTimeout(() => setCopied(false), 2000);
  };

  const download = () => {
    if (!result) return;
    const blob = new Blob([result.lockspecText], { type: "text/markdown" });
    const a = document.createElement("a");
    a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    a.download = `${result.sourceName.replace(/\s+/g,"-").toLowerCase()}.lockspec.md`;
    a.click();
  };

  const totalTokens = stages.reduce((s,st) => s + st.tokens, 0);

  return (
    <div style={{
      height: "100%", display: "flex", flexDirection: "column",
      background: "#06000f", color: "#fef0f7", fontFamily: "'DM Sans', sans-serif",
      overflow: "auto", padding: "24px",
    }}>
      {/* Header */}
      <div style={{ marginBottom: 24 }}>
        <h1 style={{ fontFamily: "'Syne', sans-serif", fontSize: 28, fontWeight: 900,
          letterSpacing: "-0.03em", color: "#ff2d6b", margin: 0 }}>
          Vision Import Pipeline
        </h1>
        <p style={{ fontSize: 12, color: "rgba(255,200,230,0.5)", marginTop: 4, fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono', monospace" }}>
          7-stage screenshot → lockspec · Gemini 2.5 Flash Vision
        </p>
      </div>

      <div style={{ display: "grid", gridTemplateColumns: "1fr 1fr", gap: 20, flex: 1, minHeight: 0 }}>
        {/* Left: upload + pipeline */}
        <div style={{ display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 16 }}>
          {/* Drop zone */}
          {!image ? (
            <div {...getRootProps()} style={{
              border: `2px dashed ${isDragActive ? "#ff2d6b" : "rgba(255,255,255,0.1)"}`,
              borderRadius: 20, padding: "48px 24px", textAlign: "center", cursor: "pointer",
              background: isDragActive ? "rgba(255,45,107,0.06)" : "rgba(255,255,255,0.02)",
              transition: "all 0.2s",
            }}>
              <input {...getInputProps()} />
              <Image size={40} style={{ color: "#ff2d6b", margin: "0 auto 12px" }} />
              <p style={{ fontWeight: 700, marginBottom: 6 }}>
                {isDragActive ? "Drop screenshot" : "Upload UI Screenshot"}
              </p>
              <p style={{ fontSize: 11, color: "rgba(255,200,230,0.4)", fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono', monospace" }}>
                PNG · JPG · WEBP · GIF
              </p>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div style={{ borderRadius: 16, overflow: "hidden", border: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.09)" }}>
              <img src={image.dataUrl} alt={image.name}
                style={{ width: "100%", maxHeight: 200, objectFit: "contain", background: "#0d0018" }} />
              <div style={{ padding: "8px 12px", display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between",
                background: "#0d0018", borderTop: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.06)" }}>
                <span style={{ fontSize: 11, color: "rgba(255,200,230,0.5)", fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono', monospace" }}>
                  {image.name}
                </span>
                <button onClick={() => setImage(null)}
                  style={{ background: "none", border: "none", cursor: "pointer", color: "#ff2d6b" }}>
                  <X size={14} />
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* Pipeline stages */}
          <div style={{ borderRadius: 16, overflow: "hidden", border: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.06)",
            background: "rgba(0,0,0,0.4)" }}>
            <div style={{ padding: "10px 14px", borderBottom: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.06)",
              fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 800, letterSpacing: "0.15em", textTransform: "uppercase",
              color: "rgba(255,200,230,0.4)", display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between" }}>
              <span>Pipeline Stages</span>
              {totalTokens > 0 && <span style={{ color: "#ffca30" }}>{totalTokens.toLocaleString()} tokens</span>}
            </div>
            {stages.map((stage, i) => (
              <div key={stage.id} style={{
                display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 12, padding: "10px 14px",
                borderBottom: i < stages.length-1 ? "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.04)" : "none",
                background: stage.status === "running" ? "rgba(255,202,48,0.04)" : "transparent",
              }}>
                <div style={{
                  width: 7, height: 7, borderRadius: "50%",
                  background: STAGE_COLOR[stage.status],
                  boxShadow: stage.status === "running" ? `0 0 8px ${STAGE_COLOR.running}` :
                    stage.status === "done" ? `0 0 8px ${STAGE_COLOR.done}` : "none",
                  animation: stage.status === "running" ? "pulse 1.2s infinite" : "none",
                  flexShrink: 0,
                }} />
                <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 700, color: "rgba(255,200,230,0.8)" }}>
                    {STAGE_LABELS[stage.id]}
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 9, color: "rgba(255,200,230,0.3)", fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono', monospace",
                    marginTop: 2 }}>
                    {stage.message}
                  </div>
                </div>
                {stage.tokens > 0 && (
                  <span style={{ fontSize: 9, fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono', monospace",
                    color: "rgba(255,200,230,0.3)" }}>
                    {stage.tokens}t
                  </span>
                )}
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>

          {error && (
            <div style={{ padding: "12px 16px", borderRadius: 12, background: "rgba(255,0,85,0.08)",
              border: "1px solid rgba(255,0,85,0.2)", fontSize: 12, color: "#ff2d6b" }}>
              {error}
            </div>
          )}

          <button
            onClick={runPipeline}
            disabled={!image || running}
            style={{
              padding: "14px 24px", borderRadius: 16, border: "none", cursor: !image||running?"not-allowed":"pointer",
              background: !image||running ? "rgba(255,255,255,0.05)" : "linear-gradient(135deg,#ff2d6b,#8b00ff)",
              color: !image||running ? "rgba(255,200,230,0.3)" : "#fff",
              fontFamily: "'Syne', sans-serif", fontWeight: 800, fontSize: 13,
              letterSpacing: "0.08em", display: "flex", alignItems: "center",
              justifyContent: "center", gap: 10,
              boxShadow: !image||running ? "none" : "0 0 24px rgba(255,45,107,0.35)",
              transition: "all 0.2s",
            }}>
            {running ? <><Loader2 size={16} style={{ animation: "spin 1s linear infinite" }} /> Running Pipeline…</> :
              <><Cpu size={16} /> Run 7-Stage Pipeline</>}
          </button>
        </div>

        {/* Right: result */}
        <div style={{ display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 16, minHeight: 0 }}>
          {result ? (
            <>
              <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "space-between" }}>
                <div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 800, color: "#00f5a0" }}>
                    ✦ {result.sourceName}
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 10, fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono', monospace",
                    color: "rgba(255,200,230,0.3)", marginTop: 2 }}>
                    {result.totalTokens.toLocaleString()} tokens · {result.lockspecText.split("\n").length} lines
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8 }}>
                  <button onClick={copy} style={{
                    padding: "6px 14px", borderRadius: 10, border: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.1)",
                    background: "rgba(255,255,255,0.04)", color: "rgba(255,200,230,0.6)",
                    cursor: "pointer", fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 700, display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6 }}>
                    {copied ? <><CheckCheck size={11} /> Copied</> : <><Copy size={11} /> Copy</>}
                  </button>
                  <button onClick={download} style={{
                    padding: "6px 14px", borderRadius: 10, border: "1px solid rgba(255,0,85,0.2)",
                    background: "rgba(255,0,85,0.06)", color: "#ff2d6b",
                    cursor: "pointer", fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 700, display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6 }}>
                    <Download size={11} /> Export .md
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>
              <div style={{ flex: 1, borderRadius: 16, overflow: "hidden",
                border: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.06)", minHeight: 0 }}>
                <div style={{ height: "100%", overflow: "auto", padding: 16,
                  background: "rgba(0,0,0,0.5)" }}>
                  <pre style={{ fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono', monospace", fontSize: 11,
                    color: "rgba(255,200,230,0.7)", whiteSpace: "pre-wrap", lineHeight: 1.6,
                    margin: 0 }}>
                    {result.lockspecText}
                  </pre>
                </div>
              </div>
            </>
          ) : (
            <div style={{ flex: 1, display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", alignItems: "center",
              justifyContent: "center", gap: 16, borderRadius: 20,
              border: "2px dashed rgba(255,255,255,0.06)" }}>
              <Sparkles size={48} style={{ color: "rgba(255,255,255,0.08)" }} />
              <div style={{ textAlign: "center" }}>
                <p style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, color: "rgba(255,200,230,0.3)", marginBottom: 4 }}>
                  Lockspec Result
                </p>
                <p style={{ fontSize: 11, color: "rgba(255,200,230,0.2)", fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono', monospace" }}>
                  Upload screenshot and run pipeline
                </p>
              </div>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      <style>{`
        @keyframes spin { to { transform: rotate(360deg); } }
        @keyframes pulse { 0%,100% { opacity:1; } 50% { opacity:0.4; } }
      `}</style>
    </div>
  );
}

'@

Write-File 'src\hooks\useChainingWorkflow.ts' @'
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { devtools } from 'zustand/middleware';

export interface WorkflowNode {
  id: string;
  type: 'vault' | 'forge' | 'simulation' | 'export' | 'analytics';
  label: string;
  position: { x: number; y: number };
  data: Record<string, any>;
  status: 'idle' | 'running' | 'completed' | 'error';
  output?: any;
  error?: string;
}

export interface WorkflowConnection {
  id: string;
  source: string;
  target: string;
  sourceOutput: string;
  targetInput: string;
}

export interface Workflow {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  description: string;
  nodes: WorkflowNode[];
  connections: WorkflowConnection[];
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
  isExecuting: boolean;
  executionHistory: Array<{
    timestamp: Date;
    status: 'success' | 'failed';
    duration: number;
    results: Record<string, any>;
  }>;
}

interface WorkflowStore {
  workflows: Workflow[];
  activeWorkflow: Workflow | null;
  selectedNode: string | null;

  // Workflow management
  createWorkflow: (name: string, description: string) => Workflow;
  deleteWorkflow: (id: string) => void;
  loadWorkflow: (id: string) => void;
  saveWorkflow: (workflow: Workflow) => void;

  // Node management
  addNode: (type: WorkflowNode['type'], position: { x: number; y: number }) => void;
  removeNode: (nodeId: string) => void;
  updateNode: (nodeId: string, data: Partial<WorkflowNode>) => void;
  selectNode: (nodeId: string | null) => void;

  // Connection management
  addConnection: (source: string, target: string, sourceOutput: string, targetInput: string) => void;
  removeConnection: (connectionId: string) => void;

  // Execution
  executeWorkflow: () => Promise<void>;
  executeNode: (nodeId: string) => Promise<void>;
  cancelExecution: () => void;

  // Utilities
  getNodeOutput: (nodeId: string) => any;
  validateWorkflow: () => boolean;
  exportWorkflow: (format: 'json' | 'yaml') => string;
  importWorkflow: (data: string, format: 'json' | 'yaml') => void;
}

export const useChainingWorkflow = create<WorkflowStore>()(
  devtools((set, get) => ({
    workflows: [],
    activeWorkflow: null,
    selectedNode: null,

    createWorkflow: (name: string, description: string) => {
      const workflow: Workflow = {
        id: `wf-${Date.now()}`,
        name,
        description,
        nodes: [],
        connections: [],
        createdAt: new Date(),
        updatedAt: new Date(),
        isExecuting: false,
        executionHistory: [],
      };

      set((state) => ({
        workflows: [...state.workflows, workflow],
        activeWorkflow: workflow,
      }));

      return workflow;
    },

    deleteWorkflow: (id: string) => {
      set((state) => ({
        workflows: state.workflows.filter((w) => w.id !== id),
        activeWorkflow: state.activeWorkflow?.id === id ? null : state.activeWorkflow,
      }));
    },

    loadWorkflow: (id: string) => {
      const workflow = get().workflows.find((w) => w.id === id);
      if (workflow) {
        set({ activeWorkflow: workflow });
      }
    },

    saveWorkflow: (workflow: Workflow) => {
      set((state) => ({
        workflows: state.workflows.map((w) => (w.id === workflow.id ? workflow : w)),
        activeWorkflow: workflow,
      }));
    },

    addNode: (type: WorkflowNode['type'], position: { x: number; y: number }) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (!state.activeWorkflow) return state;

        const newNode: WorkflowNode = {
          id: `node-${Date.now()}`,
          type,
          label: `${type.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + type.slice(1)} ${state.activeWorkflow.nodes.length + 1}`,
          position,
          data: {},
          status: 'idle',
        };

        return {
          activeWorkflow: {
            ...state.activeWorkflow,
            nodes: [...state.activeWorkflow.nodes, newNode],
            updatedAt: new Date(),
          },
        };
      });
    },

    removeNode: (nodeId: string) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (!state.activeWorkflow) return state;

        return {
          activeWorkflow: {
            ...state.activeWorkflow,
            nodes: state.activeWorkflow.nodes.filter((n) => n.id !== nodeId),
            connections: state.activeWorkflow.connections.filter(
              (c) => c.source !== nodeId && c.target !== nodeId
            ),
            updatedAt: new Date(),
          },
        };
      });
    },

    updateNode: (nodeId: string, data: Partial<WorkflowNode>) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (!state.activeWorkflow) return state;

        return {
          activeWorkflow: {
            ...state.activeWorkflow,
            nodes: state.activeWorkflow.nodes.map((n) =>
              n.id === nodeId ? { ...n, ...data } : n
            ),
            updatedAt: new Date(),
          },
        };
      });
    },

    selectNode: (nodeId: string | null) => {
      set({ selectedNode: nodeId });
    },

    addConnection: (source: string, target: string, sourceOutput: string, targetInput: string) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (!state.activeWorkflow) return state;

        const connection: WorkflowConnection = {
          id: `conn-${Date.now()}`,
          source,
          target,
          sourceOutput,
          targetInput,
        };

        return {
          activeWorkflow: {
            ...state.activeWorkflow,
            connections: [...state.activeWorkflow.connections, connection],
            updatedAt: new Date(),
          },
        };
      });
    },

    removeConnection: (connectionId: string) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (!state.activeWorkflow) return state;

        return {
          activeWorkflow: {
            ...state.activeWorkflow,
            connections: state.activeWorkflow.connections.filter((c) => c.id !== connectionId),
            updatedAt: new Date(),
          },
        };
      });
    },

    executeWorkflow: async () => {
      const state = get();
      if (!state.activeWorkflow) return;

      set((s) => ({
        activeWorkflow: s.activeWorkflow ? { ...s.activeWorkflow, isExecuting: true } : null,
      }));

      try {
        const startTime = Date.now();
        const results: Record<string, any> = {};

        // Execute nodes in topological order
        for (const node of state.activeWorkflow.nodes) {
          await get().executeNode(node.id);
        }

        const duration = Date.now() - startTime;

        set((s) => ({
          activeWorkflow: s.activeWorkflow
            ? {
                ...s.activeWorkflow,
                isExecuting: false,
                executionHistory: [
                  ...s.activeWorkflow.executionHistory,
                  {
                    timestamp: new Date(),
                    status: 'success',
                    duration,
                    results,
                  },
                ],
              }
            : null,
        }));
      } catch (error) {
        set((s) => ({
          activeWorkflow: s.activeWorkflow
            ? {
                ...s.activeWorkflow,
                isExecuting: false,
                executionHistory: [
                  ...s.activeWorkflow.executionHistory,
                  {
                    timestamp: new Date(),
                    status: 'failed',
                    duration: 0,
                    results: { error: String(error) },
                  },
                ],
              }
            : null,
        }));
      }
    },

    executeNode: async (nodeId: string) => {
      const state = get();
      if (!state.activeWorkflow) return;

      const node = state.activeWorkflow.nodes.find((n) => n.id === nodeId);
      if (!node) return;

      get().updateNode(nodeId, { status: 'running' });

      try {
        // Simulate node execution
        await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));

        get().updateNode(nodeId, {
          status: 'completed',
          output: { result: 'success', timestamp: new Date() },
        });
      } catch (error) {
        get().updateNode(nodeId, {
          status: 'error',
          error: String(error),
        });
      }
    },

    cancelExecution: () => {
      set((state) => ({
        activeWorkflow: state.activeWorkflow
          ? { ...state.activeWorkflow, isExecuting: false }
          : null,
      }));
    },

    getNodeOutput: (nodeId: string) => {
      const state = get();
      const node = state.activeWorkflow?.nodes.find((n) => n.id === nodeId);
      return node?.output;
    },

    validateWorkflow: () => {
      const state = get();
      if (!state.activeWorkflow) return false;

      // Check if all nodes have inputs
      for (const node of state.activeWorkflow.nodes) {
        if (node.type === 'forge' && !node.data.slot1) return false;
      }

      return true;
    },

    exportWorkflow: (format: 'json' | 'yaml') => {
      const state = get();
      if (!state.activeWorkflow) return '';

      if (format === 'json') {
        return JSON.stringify(state.activeWorkflow, null, 2);
      }

      // Simple YAML export
      return `name: ${state.activeWorkflow.name}\ndescription: ${state.activeWorkflow.description}\nnodes: ${state.activeWorkflow.nodes.length}`;
    },

    importWorkflow: (data: string, format: 'json' | 'yaml') => {
      try {
        if (format === 'json') {
          const workflow = JSON.parse(data) as Workflow;
          set((state) => ({
            workflows: [...state.workflows, workflow],
            activeWorkflow: workflow,
          }));
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Failed to import workflow:', error);
      }
    },
  }))
);

'@

Write-File 'src\hooks\useForge.ts' @'
import { useState, useCallback } from "react";
import type { VaultFile } from "./useVault";

export interface EvolutionResult {
  newSystemName: string; featureType: string; evolutionScore: number;
  logicExplanation: string; evolvedContent: string;
  migrationNotes: string; breakingChanges: string;
  blueprintName: string; matrixName: string; appliedAbility: string;
  timestamp: string;
}

export function useForge() {
  const [blueprintId, setBlueprintId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [matrixId, setMatrixId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [ability, setAbility] = useState("");
  const [result, setResult] = useState<EvolutionResult | null>(null);
  const [history, setHistory] = useState<EvolutionResult[]>([]);
  const [running, setRunning] = useState(false);
  const [busyMsg, setBusyMsg] = useState("");

  const evolve = useCallback(async (files: VaultFile[]) => {
    const bp = files.find(f => f.id === blueprintId);
    const mx = files.find(f => f.id === matrixId);
    if (!bp || !mx || !ability || blueprintId === matrixId) return;

    setRunning(true);
    setBusyMsg("Initiating evolution…");
    try {
      const res = await fetch("/api/ai/evolve", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          blueprintName: bp.name,
          blueprintContent: bp.content ?? "[binary asset]",
          blueprintPurpose: bp.analysis?.corePurpose ?? "",
          matrixName: mx.name,
          ability,
        }),
      });
      const data = await res.json() as EvolutionResult & { error?: string };
      if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
      const full: EvolutionResult = { ...data,
        blueprintName: bp.name, matrixName: mx.name,
        appliedAbility: ability, timestamp: new Date().toISOString() };
      setResult(full);
      setHistory(prev => [full, ...prev.slice(0, 49)]);
    } catch (e: unknown) {
      throw e;
    } finally {
      setRunning(false);
      setBusyMsg("");
    }
  }, [blueprintId, matrixId, ability]);

  return {
    blueprintId, matrixId, ability, result, history, running, busyMsg,
    setBlueprintId, setMatrixId, setAbility,
    setResult, evolve,
    clearResult: () => setResult(null),
    clearHistory: () => setHistory([]),
  };
}

'@

Write-File 'src\hooks\useGeminiStream.ts' @'
import { useState, useRef, useCallback } from "react";

interface Message { role: "user" | "ai"; content: string; time: string }

export function useGeminiStream() {
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>([]);
  const [streaming, setStreaming] = useState(false);
  const [streamText, setStreamText] = useState("");
  const abortRef = useRef<AbortController | null>(null);

  const send = useCallback(async (
    prompt: string,
    systemPrompt?: string,
    imageBase64?: string,
    imageMime?: string
  ) => {
    if (streaming) return;
    const userMsg: Message = { role: "user", content: prompt, time: new Date().toLocaleTimeString() };
    setMessages(prev => [...prev, userMsg]);
    setStreaming(true);
    setStreamText("");
    abortRef.current = new AbortController();
    let aiText = "";

    try {
      if (imageBase64 && imageMime) {
        const res = await fetch("/api/ai/vision", {
          method: "POST",
          headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
          body: JSON.stringify({ prompt, imageBase64, mimeType: imageMime }),
          signal: abortRef.current.signal,
        });
        const data = await res.json() as { text?: string; error?: string };
        if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
        aiText = data.text ?? "";
        setStreamText(aiText);
      } else {
        const history = messages.map(m => ({ role: m.role === "ai" ? "model" : "user", parts: [{ text: m.content }] }));
        const res = await fetch("/api/ai", {
          method: "POST",
          headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
          body: JSON.stringify({ prompt, stream: true, systemPrompt, history }),
          signal: abortRef.current.signal,
        });
        if (!res.ok || !res.body) throw new Error("Stream failed");
        const reader = res.body.getReader();
        const dec = new TextDecoder();
        while (true) {
          const { done, value } = await reader.read();
          if (done) break;
          for (const line of dec.decode(value).split("\n")) {
            if (line.startsWith("data: ")) {
              const payload = line.slice(6).trim();
              if (payload === "[DONE]") break;
              try {
                const d = JSON.parse(payload) as { text?: string; error?: string };
                if (d.text) { aiText += d.text; setStreamText(aiText); }
              } catch { /* skip */ }
            }
          }
        }
      }
      setMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: "ai", content: aiText, time: new Date().toLocaleTimeString() }]);
    } catch (e: unknown) {
      if ((e as Error).name !== "AbortError") {
        const msg = e instanceof Error ? e.message : "Request failed";
        setMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: "ai", content: `⚠️ ${msg}`, time: new Date().toLocaleTimeString() }]);
      }
    } finally {
      setStreaming(false);
      setStreamText("");
    }
  }, [messages, streaming]);

  const stop = useCallback(() => { abortRef.current?.abort(); setStreaming(false); setStreamText(""); }, []);
  const clear = useCallback(() => setMessages([]), []);

  return { messages, streaming, streamText, send, stop, clear };
}

Write-File 'src\hooks\useVault.ts' @'
import { useState, useCallback } from "react";

export interface VaultFile {
  id: string; name: string; ext: string; mime: string; size: number;
  kind: "text" | "image" | "binary";
  content: string | null; base64: string | null; dataUrl: string | null;
  analysis: { corePurpose: string; dataType: string; abilities: string[] } | null;
  status: "pending" | "analyzing" | "done" | "error";
  error: string | null;
  ts: string;
}

const TEXT_EXTS = new Set(["txt","md","json","csv","js","ts","jsx","tsx","html","css",
  "xml","yaml","yml","sql","py","go","rs","sh","ps1","vue","svelte"]);
const IMAGE_EXTS = new Set(["png","jpg","jpeg","webp","gif","svg","bmp"]);

async function readFile(file: File): Promise<{ content: string | null; base64: string | null; dataUrl: string | null; kind: VaultFile["kind"] }> {
  const ext = (file.name.split(".").pop() || "").toLowerCase();
  if (TEXT_EXTS.has(ext)) {
    const content = await file.text();
    return { content, base64: null, dataUrl: null, kind: "text" };
  }
  if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext) || file.type.startsWith("image/")) {
    const dataUrl = await new Promise<string>((res, rej) => {
      const r = new FileReader();
      r.onload = () => res(r.result as string);
      r.onerror = rej;
      r.readAsDataURL(file);
    });
    const base64 = dataUrl.split(",")[1];
    return { content: null, base64, dataUrl, kind: "image" };
  }
  return { content: null, base64: null, dataUrl: null, kind: "binary" };
}

export function useVault() {
  const [files, setFiles] = useState<VaultFile[]>([]);
  const [importing, setImporting] = useState(false);

  const addFile = useCallback(async (file: File) => {
    setImporting(true);
    const id = Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 10);
    const ext = (file.name.split(".").pop() || "").toLowerCase();
    const { content, base64, dataUrl, kind } = await readFile(file);

    const vf: VaultFile = {
      id, name: file.name, ext, mime: file.type || "application/octet-stream",
      size: file.size, kind, content, base64, dataUrl,
      analysis: null, status: "analyzing", error: null,
      ts: new Date().toLocaleTimeString("th-TH", { hour: "2-digit", minute: "2-digit" }),
    };
    setFiles(prev => [vf, ...prev]);

    try {
      const res = await fetch("/api/ai/analyze", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ name: file.name, content: content ?? undefined,
          imageBase64: base64 ?? undefined, mimeType: file.type || undefined }),
      });
      const analysis = await res.json() as { corePurpose: string; dataType: string; abilities: string[] };
      setFiles(prev => prev.map(f => f.id === id ? { ...f, analysis, status: "done" } : f));
    } catch (e: unknown) {
      const msg = e instanceof Error ? e.message : "Analysis failed";
      setFiles(prev => prev.map(f => f.id === id ? { ...f, status: "error", error: msg } : f));
    } finally {
      setImporting(false);
    }
  }, []);

  const removeFile = useCallback((id: string) => {
    setFiles(prev => prev.filter(f => f.id !== id));
  }, []);

  const clearAll = useCallback(() => setFiles([]), []);

  return { files, importing, addFile, removeFile, clearAll };
}

Write-File 'src\lib\gemini\client.ts' @'
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  GEMINI CLIENT v3.0 — OMEGA ULTRA
//  Features: Exponential backoff (v26), streaming SSE, vision, JSON
//  Model: gemini-2.5-flash-preview-04-17 (latest)
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
import { GoogleGenAI } from "@google/genai";

export const GEMINI_MODEL     = "gemini-2.5-flash-preview-04-17";
export const GEMINI_MODEL_ALT = "gemini-2.0-flash";
const MAX_RETRIES = 5;
const BACKOFF_BASE_MS = 800;

function getApiKey(): string {
  const key = process.env.GEMINI_API_KEY;
  if (!key) throw new Error("GEMINI_API_KEY not configured");
  return key;
}

// ─── Exponential backoff wrapper (from v26-OMEGA) ───────────────
async function withBackoff<T>(fn: () => Promise<T>, retries = MAX_RETRIES): Promise<T> {
  for (let i = 0; i < retries; i++) {
    try {
      return await fn();
    } catch (err: unknown) {
      const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
      const isRetryable = /rate.limit|quota|503|429|overloaded/i.test(msg);
      if (!isRetryable || i === retries - 1) throw err;
      const delay = BACKOFF_BASE_MS * Math.pow(2, i) + Math.random() * 400;
      console.warn(\`Gemini retry \${i+1}/\${retries} in \${Math.round(delay)}ms: \${msg}\`);
      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, delay));
    }
  }
  throw new Error("Max retries exceeded");
}

// ─── System instruction ────────────────────────────────────────
const SYSTEM_DEFAULT =
  "You are WhisperX Nexus Omega — an elite AI assistant for a high-fidelity " +
  "knowledge evolution platform. You help with code synthesis, document analysis, " +
  "architecture design, project management, and canvas-based visualization. " +
  "Be precise, technical, and exhaustive. Gemini 2.5 Flash at full capacity.";

// ─── One-shot completion ───────────────────────────────────────
export async function geminiComplete(
  prompt: string,
  systemPrompt = SYSTEM_DEFAULT,
  opts?: { temperature?: number; maxTokens?: number; model?: string }
): Promise<string> {
  return withBackoff(async () => {
    const ai = new GoogleGenAI({ apiKey: getApiKey() });
    const resp = await ai.models.generateContent({
      model: opts?.model ?? GEMINI_MODEL,
      contents: [{ role: "user", parts: [{ text: prompt }] }],
      config: {
        systemInstruction: systemPrompt,
        temperature: opts?.temperature ?? 0.7,
        topP: 0.95,
        maxOutputTokens: opts?.maxTokens ?? 8192,
      },
    });
    return resp.text ?? "";
  });
}

// ─── Streaming (returns SSE reader) ───────────────────────────
export async function geminiStream(
  prompt: string,
  systemPrompt = SYSTEM_DEFAULT,
  history?: Array<{ role: string; parts: { text: string }[] }>
): Promise<AsyncIterable<string>> {
  const ai = new GoogleGenAI({ apiKey: getApiKey() });
  const contents = [...(history ?? []), { role: "user", parts: [{ text: prompt }] }];
  const stream = await ai.models.generateContentStream({
    model: GEMINI_MODEL,
    contents,
    config: { systemInstruction: systemPrompt, temperature: 0.7, maxOutputTokens: 8192 },
  });
  return (async function* () {
    for await (const chunk of stream) {
      const text = chunk.text ?? "";
      if (text) yield text;
    }
  })();
}

// ─── Vision (multimodal) ───────────────────────────────────────
export async function geminiVision(
  prompt: string,
  imageBase64: string,
  mimeType = "image/jpeg",
  opts?: { temperature?: number }
): Promise<string> {
  return withBackoff(async () => {
    const ai = new GoogleGenAI({ apiKey: getApiKey() });
    const resp = await ai.models.generateContent({
      model: GEMINI_MODEL,
      contents: [{
        role: "user",
        parts: [
          { inlineData: { mimeType, data: imageBase64 } },
          { text: prompt },
        ],
      }],
      config: {
        systemInstruction: "You are a precise visual analysis engine. Extract all information accurately.",
        temperature: opts?.temperature ?? 0.2,
        maxOutputTokens: 4096,
      },
    });
    return resp.text ?? "";
  });
}

// ─── JSON extraction ───────────────────────────────────────────
export async function geminiJSON<T>(
  prompt: string,
  fallback: T,
  systemPrompt?: string
): Promise<T> {
  const text = await geminiComplete(
    prompt,
    systemPrompt ?? "Return ONLY valid JSON, no markdown, no preamble.",
    { temperature: 0.1 }
  );
  try {
    return JSON.parse(text.replace(/```json\s*/gi, "").replace(/```\s*/g, "").trim()) as T;
  } catch {
    return fallback;
  }
}

// ─── Analysis (v26 logic extraction) ──────────────────────────
export async function geminiAnalyze(
  name: string,
  content: string,
  imageBase64?: string,
  mimeType?: string
): Promise<{ corePurpose: string; dataType: string; abilities: string[] }> {
  const sys = \`Logic extraction engine v3.0. Return ONLY valid JSON:
{"corePurpose":"one sharp sentence","dataType":"type label","abilities":["Label: description","Label: description","Label: description"]}\`;

  let text: string;
  if (imageBase64 && mimeType?.startsWith("image/")) {
    text = await geminiVision(
      \`Analyze file: \${name}\n\nExtract production logic. Return JSON only.\`,
      imageBase64, mimeType, { temperature: 0.1 }
    );
  } else {
    text = await geminiComplete(
      \`Analyze file: "\${name}"\n\nContent:\n\${(content || "").slice(0, 15000)}\`,
      sys, { temperature: 0.1, maxTokens: 512 }
    );
  }
  try {
    return JSON.parse(text.replace(/```json\s*/gi, "").replace(/```/g, "").trim());
  } catch {
    return { corePurpose: "Asset with extractable logic", dataType: "binary", abilities: [] };
  }
}

// ─── Evolution engine (v26 aiEvolve) ──────────────────────────
export async function geminiEvolve(opts: {
  blueprintName: string;
  blueprintContent: string;
  blueprintPurpose: string;
  matrixName: string;
  ability: string;
}): Promise<{
  newSystemName: string; featureType: string; evolutionScore: number;
  logicExplanation: string; evolvedContent: string;
  migrationNotes: string; breakingChanges: string;
}> {
  const sys = \`You are Zenith Evolution Engine Omega v3.0.
Return ONLY valid JSON:
{"newSystemName":"string","featureType":"SYNTHESIS|ENHANCEMENT|FUSION|UPGRADE",
"evolutionScore":98,"logicExplanation":"2 precise sentences",
"migrationNotes":"deployment steps","breakingChanges":"none or list",
"evolvedContent":"COMPLETE PRODUCTION OUTPUT — min 500 chars"}\`;

  const prompt = \`BLUEPRINT: "\${opts.blueprintName}" (Purpose: \${opts.blueprintPurpose})
CONTENT:
\${opts.blueprintContent.slice(0, 8000)}

MATRIX: "\${opts.matrixName}"
ABILITY: "\${opts.ability}"

Produce complete evolved production output now.\`;

  return withBackoff(async () => {
    const ai = new GoogleGenAI({ apiKey: getApiKey() });
    const resp = await ai.models.generateContent({
      model: GEMINI_MODEL,
      contents: [{ role: "user", parts: [{ text: prompt }] }],
      config: { systemInstruction: sys, temperature: 0.5, maxOutputTokens: 16384 },
    });
    const text = (resp.text ?? "").replace(/```json\s*/gi, "").replace(/```/g, "").trim();
    return JSON.parse(text);
  });
}

import { type ClassValue, clsx } from "clsx";
import { twMerge } from "tailwind-merge";

export const cn = (...i: ClassValue[]) => twMerge(clsx(i));

export const uid = () => Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 11);

export const fmt = (bytes: number): string =>
  bytes > 1e6 ? `${(bytes/1e6).toFixed(1)} MB`
  : bytes > 1e3 ? `${Math.round(bytes/1e3)} KB`
  : `${bytes} B`;

export const fmtCurrency = (v: number, currency = "THB") =>
  new Intl.NumberFormat("th-TH", { style: "currency", currency, maximumFractionDigits: 0 }).format(v);

export const fmtDate = (d: string | Date) =>
  new Intl.DateTimeFormat("th-TH", { day: "numeric", month: "short", year: "numeric" }).format(new Date(d));

export const relativeTime = (ts: number): string => {
  const diff = Date.now() - ts;
  const m = Math.floor(diff / 60000);
  if (m < 1) return "just now";
  if (m < 60) return `${m}m ago`;
  const h = Math.floor(m / 60);
  if (h < 24) return `${h}h ago`;
  return `${Math.floor(h/24)}d ago`;
};

export const clamp = (n: number, min: number, max: number) =>
  Math.max(min, Math.min(max, n));

export const sleep = (ms: number) => new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, ms));

// File extension color mapping (v26 FILE_REGISTRY)

};

  EXT_COLOR[ext?.toUpperCase()] ?? "rgba(180,188,220,0.25)";

// Canvas helpers
export const screenToCanvas = (
  clientX: number, clientY: number,
  containerRect: DOMRect,
  pan: { x: number; y: number }, zoom: number
) => ({
  x: (clientX - containerRect.left - pan.x) / zoom,
  y: (clientY - containerRect.top - pan.y) / zoom,
});

Write-File 'src\lib\vision\pipeline.ts' @'
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  VISION IMPORT PIPELINE — 7-Stage Screenshot → LockSpec
//  Source: Visionp.txt reference implementation
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
import { geminiVision, geminiJSON } from "@/lib/gemini/client";

export type VisionStageStatus = "idle" | "running" | "done" | "error";

export interface VisionStageState {
  id:      string;
  status:  VisionStageStatus;
  message: string;
  tokens:  number;
}

export type SourceType = "lockspec" | "feature_spec" | "implementation_plan" | "vision_import";

export interface StructuralSignals {
  headings:         string[];
  bullets:          string[];
  codeBlocks:       string[];
  filePaths:        string[];
  routeHints:       string[];
  menuHints:        string[];
  configPairs:      Array<{ key: string; value: string }>;
  destructiveHints: string[];
  commands:         string[];
}

export interface VisionImportResult {
  sourceName:   string;
  detectedType: SourceType;
  confidence:   number;
  lockspecText: string;
  signals:      StructuralSignals;
  stages:       VisionStageState[];
  totalTokens:  number;
}

export const PIPELINE_STAGES: VisionStageState[] = [
  { id: "blueprint", status: "idle", message: "Waiting…", tokens: 0 },
  { id: "tokens",    status: "idle", message: "Waiting…", tokens: 0 },
  { id: "patterns",  status: "idle", message: "Waiting…", tokens: 0 },
  { id: "codegen",   status: "idle", message: "Waiting…", tokens: 0 },
  { id: "rules",     status: "idle", message: "Waiting…", tokens: 0 },
  { id: "refine",    status: "idle", message: "Waiting…", tokens: 0 },
  { id: "export",    status: "idle", message: "Waiting…", tokens: 0 },
];

export function advanceStage(
  stages:  VisionStageState[],
  id:      string,
  status:  VisionStageStatus,
  message: string,
  tokens = 0
): VisionStageState[] {
  return stages.map(s => s.id === id ? { ...s, status, message, tokens } : s);
}

export async function runVisionImportPipeline(
  imageBase64:    string,
  imageMimeType:  string,
  onProgress:     (stages: VisionStageState[]) => void
): Promise<VisionImportResult> {
  let stages = [...PIPELINE_STAGES];
  let totalTokens = 0;

  // Stage 1: Blueprint
  stages = advanceStage(stages, "blueprint", "running", "Analyzing page structure…");
  onProgress(stages);
  const blueprintPrompt = \`Analyze this UI screenshot. Return ONLY JSON:
{"title":"page title or app name","layout":"dashboard|form|landing|list|detail|editor|wizard|other",
"sections":["named sections visible in the screenshot"],"components":["component names: navbar, sidebar, hero, card, table, form, modal, footer, ..."],
"description":"one sentence describing what this UI does and who uses it"}\`;
  const blueprintRaw = await geminiVision(blueprintPrompt, imageBase64, imageMimeType, { temperature: 0.1 });
  const blueprint = JSON.parse(blueprintRaw.replace(/\`\`\`json\s*/gi,"").replace(/\`\`\`/g,"").trim()) as {
    title: string; layout: string; sections: string[]; components: string[]; description: string;
  };
  stages = advanceStage(stages, "blueprint", "done", \`\${blueprint.layout} layout detected\`, 600);
  totalTokens += 600;
  onProgress(stages);

  // Stage 2: Tokens
  stages = advanceStage(stages, "tokens", "running", "Extracting design tokens…");
  onProgress(stages);
  const tokenPrompt = \`Extract design tokens from this UI screenshot. Return ONLY JSON:
{"colors":{"primary":"#hex","secondary":"#hex","bg":"#hex","surface":"#hex","text":"#hex","muted":"#hex","border":"#hex","success":"#hex","warning":"#hex","danger":"#hex"},
"fonts":["font family names visible or inferred"],"spacing":"tight|normal|spacious","radius":"none|sm|md|lg|xl|full"}\`;
  const tokensRaw = await geminiVision(tokenPrompt, imageBase64, imageMimeType, { temperature: 0.1 });
  const tokens = JSON.parse(tokensRaw.replace(/\`\`\`json\s*/gi,"").replace(/\`\`\`/g,"").trim()) as {
    colors: Record<string,string>; fonts: string[]; spacing: string; radius: string;
  };
  stages = advanceStage(stages, "tokens", "done", "Design tokens extracted", 300);
  totalTokens += 300;
  onProgress(stages);

  // Stage 3: Patterns
  stages = advanceStage(stages, "patterns", "running", "Matching UI patterns…");
  onProgress(stages);
  const patternPrompt = \`Identify UI patterns and extract lockspec signals from this screenshot. Return ONLY JSON:
{"patterns":["navbar","sidebar","hero","card_grid","stats_row","data_table","form","modal","tabs","breadcrumbs","search_bar","filter_panel","timeline","kanban","code_block","markdown_viewer","chat_interface","footer"],
"signals":{"routes":["/path/to/route"],"menus":["menu item label"],"filePaths":["path/to/file.ts"],"commands":["npm run ..."],"configPairs":[{"key":"ENV_VAR","value":"value"}],"destructive":["delete","reset","wipe"]}}\`;
  const patternsRaw = await geminiVision(patternPrompt, imageBase64, imageMimeType, { temperature: 0.1 });
  const patterns = JSON.parse(patternsRaw.replace(/\`\`\`json\s*/gi,"").replace(/\`\`\`/g,"").trim()) as {
    patterns: string[];
    signals: { routes: string[]; menus: string[]; filePaths: string[]; commands: string[]; configPairs: Array<{key:string;value:string}>; destructive: string[]; };
  };
  stages = advanceStage(stages, "patterns", "done", \`\${patterns.patterns.length} patterns found\`, 800);
  totalTokens += 800;
  onProgress(stages);

  // Stage 4: Codegen (implicit)
  stages = advanceStage(stages, "codegen", "running", "Generating structure…");
  onProgress(stages);
  await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 100));
  stages = advanceStage(stages, "codegen", "done", "Structure generated", 0);
  onProgress(stages);

  // Stage 5: Rules (implicit)
  stages = advanceStage(stages, "rules", "running", "Applying rules…");
  onProgress(stages);
  await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 80));
  stages = advanceStage(stages, "rules", "done", "Rules applied", 0);
  onProgress(stages);

  // Stage 6: Refine — Lockspec synthesis
  stages = advanceStage(stages, "refine", "running", "Synthesizing lockspec…");
  onProgress(stages);
  const refinePrompt = \`You are generating a structured lockspec from a UI screenshot.

Context:
- Title: \${blueprint.title}
- Layout: \${blueprint.layout}
- Sections: \${blueprint.sections.join(", ")}
- Components: \${blueprint.components.join(", ")}
- Patterns: \${patterns.patterns.join(", ")}
- Primary color: \${tokens.colors?.primary}
- Background: \${tokens.colors?.bg}
- Fonts: \${tokens.fonts.join(", ")}
- Spacing: \${tokens.spacing}, Radius: \${tokens.radius}

Generate a comprehensive lockspec markdown document:
1. ## Overview — purpose, users, capabilities
2. ## Component Requirements — props, states, constraints
3. ## Route & Navigation Structure
4. ## Data & State Requirements
5. ## Design Token Constraints
6. ## Implementation Rules (MUST/MUST NOT)
7. ## AI Integration Points

Return ONLY JSON:
{"lockspecText":"# LOCKSPEC\\n\\n## Overview\\n...","sourceName":"descriptive name",
"detectedType":"lockspec|feature_spec|implementation_plan|vision_import",
"confidence":0.85,"headings":["heading text"],"bullets":["bullet text"]}\`;
  const lockspecRaw = await geminiVision(refinePrompt, imageBase64, imageMimeType, { temperature: 0.2 });
  const lockspecResult = JSON.parse(lockspecRaw.replace(/\`\`\`json\s*/gi,"").replace(/\`\`\`/g,"").trim()) as {
    lockspecText: string; sourceName: string; detectedType: string; confidence: number;
    headings: string[]; bullets: string[];
  };
  stages = advanceStage(stages, "refine", "done", "Lockspec synthesized", 3000);
  totalTokens += 3000;
  onProgress(stages);

  // Stage 7: Export
  stages = advanceStage(stages, "export", "running", "Packaging result…");
  onProgress(stages);
  const signals: StructuralSignals = {
    headings:         lockspecResult.headings || [],
    bullets:          lockspecResult.bullets || [],
    codeBlocks:       [],
    filePaths:        patterns.signals.filePaths || [],
    routeHints:       patterns.signals.routes || [],
    menuHints:        patterns.signals.menus || [],
    configPairs:      patterns.signals.configPairs || [],
    destructiveHints: patterns.signals.destructive || [],
    commands:         patterns.signals.commands || [],
  };
  stages = advanceStage(stages, "export", "done", \`Pipeline complete — \${totalTokens} tokens\`, 0);
  onProgress(stages);

  return {
    sourceName:   lockspecResult.sourceName || blueprint.title,
    detectedType: lockspecResult.detectedType as SourceType || "vision_import",
    confidence:   lockspecResult.confidence || 0.85,
    lockspecText: lockspecResult.lockspecText || "",
    signals,
    stages,
    totalTokens,
  };
}

Write-File 'src\store\index.ts' @'
import { create } from "zustand"
import { persist, createJSONStorage } from "zustand/middleware"
import { immer } from "zustand/middleware/immer"
import type {
  AppMode, CanvasMode, ModuleId,
  CanvasNode, CanvasEdge, CanvasState, CanvasViewport,
  WhiteboardStroke, WhiteboardShape, WhiteboardTool,
  MermaidConfig,
  Task, Presentation, Slide, ChartConfig, CollabDoc, Proposal,
  Project, Workspace, WorkspaceSettings,
  AIProvider, AIMessage
} from "@/types"
import { uid, validateArray, safeJsonParse, safeJsonStringify, COLORS, NODE_TEMPLATES } from "@/lib/utils"

// ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  HISTORY MANAGEMENT — UNDO/REDO WITH LIMIT
// ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

interface HistoryState<T> {
  past: T[]
  future: T[]
  max: number
  push: (state: T) => void
  undo: () => T | undefined
  redo: () => T | undefined
  canUndo: boolean
  canRedo: boolean
}

function createHistory<T>(max: number = 20): HistoryState<T> {
  return {
    past: [],
    future: [],
    max,
    push(state: T) {
      this.past.push(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(state)))
      if (this.past.length > this.max) this.past.shift()
      this.future = []
    },
    undo() {
      if (this.past.length === 0) return undefined
      const current = this.past.pop()
      if (current) {
        this.future.push(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(current)))
        return current
      }
      return undefined
    },
    redo() {
      if (this.future.length === 0) return undefined
      const next = this.future.pop()
      if (next) {
        this.past.push(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(next)))
        return next
      }
      return undefined
    },
    get canUndo() { return this.past.length > 0 },
    get canRedo() { return this.future.length > 0 }
  }
}
