    { id: uid("edge"), source: "node-", target: "node-", label: "outputs" }
  ],
  viewport: { x: 0, y: 0, zoom: 1 },
  selectedIds: [],
  clipboard: null,
  history: { past: [], future: [], max: 20 }
}

// Fix edge references after node creation (safety)
function fixEdgeReferences(state: CanvasState): CanvasState {
  if (!validateArray(state.nodes) || state.nodes.length < 2) return state
  
  const nodeIds = state.nodes.map(n => n?.id).filter(Boolean) as string[]
  const edges = (state.edges || []).map((edge, i) => {
    if (!edge) return edge
    return {
      ...edge,
      source: nodeIds[Math.min(i, nodeIds.length - 2)] || edge.source,
      target: nodeIds[Math.min(i + 1, nodeIds.length - 1)] || edge.target
    }
  })
  
  return { ...state, edges }
}

// ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  MAIN STORE — APP STATE + ALL MODULES + CANVAS + AI
// ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

interface AppState {
  // ═════ APP NAVIGATION ═════
  appMode: AppMode
  activeModule: ModuleId
  canvasMode: CanvasMode
  sidebarOpen: boolean
  rightPanelOpen: boolean
  
  // ═════ PROJECTS & WORKSPACE ═════
  activeProjectId: string | null
  projects: Project[]
  workspace: Workspace
  
  // ═════ CANVAS STATE ═════
  canvasState: CanvasState
  
  // ═════ WHITEBOARD STATE ═════
  whiteboardStrokes: WhiteboardStroke[]
  whiteboardShapes: WhiteboardShape[]
  whiteboardTool: WhiteboardTool
  strokeColor: string
  strokeWidth: number
  
  // ═════ MERMAID STATE ═════
  mermaidCode: string
  mermaidConfig: MermaidConfig
  mermaidPreview: string
  
  // ═════ MODULE DATA ═════
  tasks: Task[]
  presentations: Presentation[]
  charts: ChartConfig[]
  collabDocs: CollabDoc[]
  proposals: Proposal[]
  
  // ═════ AI STATE ═════
  aiProvider: AIProvider
  aiConversations: Record<string, AIMessage[]>
  currentAIContext: { nodeId?: string; module?: string; data?: any }
  
  // ═════ UI STATE ═════
  theme: "dark" | "light" | "system"
  notifications: Array<{
    id: string
    title: string
    message: string
    type: "info" | "success" | "error" | "warning"
    timestamp: string
    read: boolean
  }>
  
  // ═════ SETTINGS ═════
  settings: WorkspaceSettings
  
  // ═════ ACTIONS — NAVIGATION ═════
  setAppMode: (mode: AppMode) => void
  setActiveModule: (id: ModuleId) => void
  setCanvasMode: (mode: CanvasMode) => void
  setSidebarOpen: (open: boolean) => void
  setRightPanelOpen: (open: boolean) => void
  
  // ═════ ACTIONS — PROJECTS ═════
  setActiveProject: (id: string | null) => void
  createProject: (name: string, mode: AppMode, canvasMode?: CanvasMode, moduleId?: ModuleId) => string
  updateProject: (id: string, patch: Partial<Project>) => void
  deleteProject: (id: string) => boolean
  exportProject: (id: string) => string | null
  importProject: (json: string) => boolean
  
  // ═════ ACTIONS — CANVAS ═════
  addNode: (node: Omit<CanvasNode, "id" | "zIndex">) => void
  updateNode: (id: string, patch: Partial<CanvasNode>) => void
  deleteNode: (id: string) => void
  addEdge: (edge: Omit<CanvasEdge, "id">) => void
  deleteEdge: (id: string) => void
  setViewport: (viewport: Partial<CanvasViewport>) => void
  setSelectedIds: (ids: string[]) => void
  copySelection: () => void
  pasteSelection: (offset?: { x: number; y: number }) => void
  undoCanvas: () => void
  redoCanvas: () => void
  clearCanvas: () => void
  exportCanvas: () => string
  importCanvas: (json: string) => boolean
  
  // ═════ ACTIONS — WHITEBOARD ═════
  addStroke: (stroke: Omit<WhiteboardStroke, "id" | "createdAt">) => void
  updateStroke: (id: string, patch: Partial<WhiteboardStroke>) => void
  deleteStroke: (id: string) => void
  addShape: (shape: Omit<WhiteboardShape, "id" | "createdAt">) => void
  updateShape: (id: string, patch: Partial<WhiteboardShape>) => void
  deleteShape: (id: string) => void
  setWhiteboardTool: (tool: WhiteboardTool) => void
  setStrokeColor: (color: string) => void
  setStrokeWidth: (width: number) => void
  clearWhiteboard: () => void
  
  // ═════ ACTIONS — MERMAID ═════
  setMermaidCode: (code: string) => void
  updateMermaidConfig: (config: Partial<MermaidConfig>) => void
  setMermaidPreview: (svg: string) => void
  
  // ═════ ACTIONS — MODULES ═════
  // Tasks
  addTask: (task: Omit<Task, "id" | "createdAt" | "updatedAt">) => void
  updateTask: (id: string, patch: Partial<Task>) => void
  deleteTask: (id: string) => void
  moveTask: (id: string, status: Task["status"]) => void
  
  // Presentations
  addPresentation: (p: Omit<Presentation, "id" | "createdAt" | "updatedAt">) => string
  updatePresentation: (id: string, patch: Partial<Presentation>) => void
  deletePresentation: (id: string) => void
  addSlide: (presentationId: string) => void
  updateSlide: (presentationId: string, slideId: string, patch: Partial<Slide>) => void
  deleteSlide: (presentationId: string, slideId: string) => void
  
  // Charts
  addChart: (chart: Omit<ChartConfig, "id" | "createdAt" | "updatedAt">) => void
  updateChart: (id: string, patch: Partial<ChartConfig>) => void
  deleteChart: (id: string) => void
  
  // Collaboration
  addCollabDoc: (doc: Omit<CollabDoc, "id" | "createdAt" | "updatedAt" | "version">) => void
  updateCollabDoc: (id: string, patch: Partial<CollabDoc>) => void
  deleteCollabDoc: (id: string) => void
  
  // Proposals
  addProposal: (p: Omit<Proposal, "id" | "createdAt" | "status">) => string
  updateProposal: (id: string, patch: Partial<Proposal>) => void
  deleteProposal: (id: string) => void
  addProposalLineItem: (proposalId: string, item: Omit<ProposalLineItem, "id">) => void
  updateProposalLineItem: (proposalId: string, itemId: string, patch: Partial<ProposalLineItem>) => void
  removeProposalLineItem: (proposalId: string, itemId: string) => void
  
  // ═════ ACTIONS — AI ═════
  setAIProvider: (provider: AIProvider) => void
  addAIMessage: (conversationId: string, message: AIMessage) => void
  clearAIConversation: (id: string) => void
  setAIContext: (context: Partial<AppState["currentAIContext"]>) => void
  
  // ═════ ACTIONS — UI ═════
  setTheme: (theme: "dark" | "light" | "system") => void
  addNotification: (n: Omit<AppState["notifications"][0], "id" | "timestamp" | "read">) => void
  markNotificationRead: (id: string) => void
  removeNotification: (id: string) => void
  updateSettings: (patch: Partial<WorkspaceSettings>) => void
}

// ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  STORE CREATION — ZUSTAND + IMMERSIVE + PERSIST
// ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

export const useAppStore = create<AppState>()(
  persist(
    immer((set, get) => ({
      // ═════ INITIAL STATE ═════
      appMode: "canvas",
      activeModule: "dashboard",
      canvasMode: "canvas",
      sidebarOpen: true,
      rightPanelOpen: true,
      
      activeProjectId: null,
      projects: [],
      workspace: {
        id: uid("ws"),
        name: "Default Workspace",
        projects: [],
        activeProjectId: null,
        settings: {
          theme: "dark",
          compactMode: false,
          showPetals: true,
          enableAnimations: true,
          defaultCanvasMode: "canvas",
          defaultModule: "dashboard",
          autoSave: true,
          confirmDelete: true,
          aiProvider: "gemini"
        },
        createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
      },
      
      canvasState: fixEdgeReferences(defaultCanvasState),
      
      whiteboardStrokes: [],
      whiteboardShapes: [],
      whiteboardTool: "select",
      strokeColor: COLORS.violet,
      strokeWidth: 3,
      
      mermaidCode: \`graph TD
  A[Start] --> B{Decision}
  B -->|Yes| C[Process]
  B -->|No| D[End]
  C --> E[Output]\`,
      mermaidConfig: { theme: "dark", flowchart: { curve: "basis" } },
      mermaidPreview: "",
      
      tasks: [],
      presentations: [],
      charts: [],
      collabDocs: [],
      proposals: [],
      
      aiProvider: "gemini",
      aiConversations: {},
      currentAIContext: {},
      
      theme: "dark",
      notifications: [],
      
      settings: {
        theme: "dark",
        compactMode: false,
        showPetals: true,
        enableAnimations: true,
        defaultCanvasMode: "canvas",
        defaultModule: "dashboard",
        autoSave: true,
        confirmDelete: true,
        aiProvider: "gemini"
      },
      
      // ═════ NAVIGATION ACTIONS ═════
      setAppMode: (mode) => set(s => { s.appMode = mode }),
      setActiveModule: (id) => set(s => { s.activeModule = id }),
      setCanvasMode: (mode) => set(s => { s.canvasMode = mode }),
      setSidebarOpen: (open) => set(s => { s.sidebarOpen = open }),
      setRightPanelOpen: (open) => set(s => { s.rightPanelOpen = open }),
      
      // ═════ PROJECT ACTIONS ═════
      setActiveProject: (id) => set(s => {
        s.activeProjectId = id
        if (id) {
          const project = s.projects.find(p => p?.id === id)
          if (project?.canvasState) s.canvasState = project.canvasState
          if (project?.whiteboardStrokes) s.whiteboardStrokes = project.whiteboardStrokes
          if (project?.whiteboardShapes) s.whiteboardShapes = project.whiteboardShapes
          if (project?.mermaidCode) s.mermaidCode = project.mermaidCode
        }
      }),
      
      createProject: (name, mode, canvasMode, moduleId) => {
        const id = uid("proj")
        const project: Project = {
          id, name, mode,
          canvasMode: mode === "canvas" ? canvasMode : undefined,
          moduleId: mode === "modules" ? moduleId : undefined,
          createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
          updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
          lastAccessed: new Date().toISOString(),
          canvasState: mode === "canvas" ? fixEdgeReferences(defaultCanvasState) : undefined,
          whiteboardStrokes: mode === "canvas" && canvasMode === "whiteboard" ? [] : undefined,
          whiteboardShapes: mode === "canvas" && canvasMode === "whiteboard" ? [] : undefined,
          mermaidCode: mode === "canvas" && canvasMode === "mermaid" ? get().mermaidCode : undefined,
          tasks: mode === "modules" && moduleId === "dashboard" ? [] : undefined,
          presentations: mode === "modules" && moduleId === "presentation" ? [] : undefined,
          charts: mode === "modules" && moduleId === "charts" ? [] : undefined,
          collabDocs: mode === "modules" && moduleId === "collaboration" ? [] : undefined,
          proposals: mode === "modules" && moduleId === "proposal" ? [] : undefined
        }
        
        set(s => {
          s.projects.unshift(project)
          s.activeProjectId = id
          s.workspace.projects = s.projects
          s.workspace.activeProjectId = id
          s.workspace.updatedAt = new Date().toISOString()
          
          // Load project data into active state
          if (project.canvasState) s.canvasState = project.canvasState
          if (project.whiteboardStrokes) s.whiteboardStrokes = project.whiteboardStrokes
          if (project.whiteboardShapes) s.whiteboardShapes = project.whiteboardShapes
          if (project.mermaidCode) s.mermaidCode = project.mermaidCode
          if (project.tasks) s.tasks = project.tasks
          if (project.presentations) s.presentations = project.presentations
          if (project.charts) s.charts = project.charts
          if (project.collabDocs) s.collabDocs = project.collabDocs
          if (project.proposals) s.proposals = project.proposals
        })
        return id
      },
      
      updateProject: (id, patch) => set(s => {
        const project = s.projects.find(p => p?.id === id)
        if (project) {
          Object.assign(project, { ...patch, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() })
          s.workspace.updatedAt = new Date().toISOString()
        }
      }),
      
      deleteProject: (id) => {
        set(s => {
          s.projects = s.projects.filter(p => p?.id !== id)
          if (s.activeProjectId === id) {
            s.activeProjectId = s.projects[0]?.id || null
          }
          s.workspace.projects = s.projects
          s.workspace.updatedAt = new Date().toISOString()
        })
        return true
      },
      
      exportProject: (id) => {
        const project = get().projects.find(p => p?.id === id)
        if (!project) return null
        return safeJsonStringify(project)
      },
      
      importProject: (json) => {
        try {
          const project = safeJsonParse<Project>(json, null)
          if (!project || !project.id) return false
          
          set(s => {
            const existing = s.projects.findIndex(p => p?.id === project.id)
            if (existing !== -1) {
              s.projects[existing] = { ...s.projects[existing], ...project }
            } else {
              s.projects.unshift(project)
            }
            s.workspace.projects = s.projects
          })
          return true
        } catch {
          return false
        }
      },
      
      // ═════ CANVAS ACTIONS ═════
      addNode: (node) => set(s => {
        if (!node || !node.type) return
        const maxZ = (s.canvasState.nodes || []).reduce((max, n) => Math.max(max, n?.zIndex || 0), 0)
        const newNode: CanvasNode = {
          ...node,
          id: uid("node"),
          zIndex: maxZ + 1,
          metadata: {
            createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
            updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
          }
        }
        s.canvasState.nodes = [...(s.canvasState.nodes || []), newNode]
        s.canvasState = fixEdgeReferences(s.canvasState)
        
        // History
        s.canvasState.history.push(s.canvasState)
      }),
      
      updateNode: (id, patch) => set(s => {
        if (!id) return
        const idx = (s.canvasState.nodes || []).findIndex(n => n?.id === id)
        if (idx !== -1 && s.canvasState.nodes[idx]) {
          Object.assign(s.canvasState.nodes[idx], {
            ...patch,
            metadata: {
              ...(s.canvasState.nodes[idx]?.metadata || {}),
              updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
            }
          })
          s.canvasState = fixEdgeReferences(s.canvasState)
        }
      }),
      
      deleteNode: (id) => set(s => {
        if (!id) return
        s.canvasState.nodes = (s.canvasState.nodes || []).filter(n => n?.id !== id)
        s.canvasState.edges = (s.canvasState.edges || []).filter(e => e?.source !== id && e?.target !== id)
        s.canvasState.selectedIds = (s.canvasState.selectedIds || []).filter(sid => sid !== id)
        s.canvasState = fixEdgeReferences(s.canvasState)
        s.canvasState.history.push(s.canvasState)
      }),
      
      addEdge: (edge) => set(s => {
        if (!edge || !edge.source || !edge.target) return
        s.canvasState.edges = [...(s.canvasState.edges || []), { ...edge, id: uid("edge") }]
        s.canvasState.history.push(s.canvasState)
      }),
      
      deleteEdge: (id) => set(s => {
        if (!id) return
        s.canvasState.edges = (s.canvasState.edges || []).filter(e => e?.id !== id)
        s.canvasState.history.push(s.canvasState)
      }),
      
      setViewport: (viewport) => set(s => {
        Object.assign(s.canvasState.viewport, viewport)
      }),
      
      setSelectedIds: (ids) => set(s => {
        s.canvasState.selectedIds = ids
      }),
      
      copySelection: () => set(s => {
        const ids = s.canvasState.selectedIds
        if (!validateArray(ids) || ids.length === 0) return
        const nodes = (s.canvasState.nodes || []).filter(n => n && ids.includes(n.id))
        const edges = (s.canvasState.edges || []).filter(e => e && ids.includes(e.source) && ids.includes(e.target))
        s.canvasState.clipboard = {
          nodes: JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(nodes)),
          edges: JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(edges))
        }
      }),
      
      pasteSelection: (offset = { x: 30, y: 30 }) => set(s => {
        if (!s.canvasState.clipboard) return
        const idMap: Record<string, string> = {}
        
        const newNodes = (s.canvasState.clipboard.nodes || []).map(n => {
          if (!n) return null
          const newId = uid("node")
          idMap[n.id] = newId
          return {
            ...n,
            id: newId,
            x: n.x + offset.x,
            y: n.y + offset.y,
            zIndex: ((s.canvasState.nodes || []).reduce((max, nd) => Math.max(max, nd?.zIndex || 0), 0) + 1),
            metadata: {
              createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
              updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
            }
          }
        }).filter(Boolean) as CanvasNode[]
        
        const newEdges = (s.canvasState.clipboard.edges || []).map(e => {
          if (!e || !idMap[e.source] || !idMap[e.target]) return null
          return { ...e, id: uid("edge"), source: idMap[e.source], target: idMap[e.target] }
        }).filter(Boolean) as CanvasEdge[]
        
        s.canvasState.nodes = [...(s.canvasState.nodes || []), ...newNodes]
        s.canvasState.edges = [...(s.canvasState.edges || []), ...newEdges]
        s.canvasState = fixEdgeReferences(s.canvasState)
        s.canvasState.history.push(s.canvasState)
      }),
      
      undoCanvas: () => set(s => {
        const prev = s.canvasState.history.undo()
        if (prev) s.canvasState = prev
      }),
      
      redoCanvas: () => set(s => {
        const next = s.canvasState.history.redo()
        if (next) s.canvasState = next
      }),
      
      clearCanvas: () => set(s => {
        s.canvasState = {
          nodes: [],
          edges: [],
          viewport: { x: 0, y: 0, zoom: 1 },
          selectedIds: [],
          clipboard: null,
          history: createHistory(20)
        }
      }),
      
      exportCanvas: () => safeJsonStringify(s.canvasState),
      
      importCanvas: (json) => {
        try {
          const data = safeJsonParse<CanvasState>(json, null)
          if (data?.nodes && data?.edges) {
            set(s => { s.canvasState = fixEdgeReferences(data) })
            return true
          }
          return false
        } catch {
          return false
        }
      },
      
      // ═════ WHITEBOARD ACTIONS ═════
      addStroke: (stroke) => set(s => {
        if (!stroke || !validateArray(stroke.points)) return
        s.whiteboardStrokes = [...s.whiteboardStrokes, {
          ...stroke,
          id: uid("stroke"),
          createdAt: new Date().toISOString()
        }]
      }),
      
      updateStroke: (id, patch) => set(s => {
        if (!id) return
        const idx = s.whiteboardStrokes.findIndex(st => st?.id === id)
        if (idx !== -1) Object.assign(s.whiteboardStrokes[idx], patch)
      }),
      
      deleteStroke: (id) => set(s => {
        if (!id) return
        s.whiteboardStrokes = s.whiteboardStrokes.filter(st => st?.id !== id)
      }),
      
      addShape: (shape) => set(s => {
        if (!shape || !shape.type) return
        s.whiteboardShapes = [...s.whiteboardShapes, {
          ...shape,
          id: uid("shape"),
          createdAt: new Date().toISOString()
        }]
      }),
      
      updateShape: (id, patch) => set(s => {
        if (!id) return
        const idx = s.whiteboardShapes.findIndex(sh => sh?.id === id)
        if (idx !== -1) Object.assign(s.whiteboardShapes[idx], patch)
      }),
      
      deleteShape: (id) => set(s => {
        if (!id) return
        s.whiteboardShapes = s.whiteboardShapes.filter(sh => sh?.id !== id)
      }),
      
      setWhiteboardTool: (tool) => set(s => { s.whiteboardTool = tool }),
      setStrokeColor: (color) => set(s => { s.strokeColor = color }),
      setStrokeWidth: (width) => set(s => { s.strokeWidth = clamp(width, 1, 20) }),
      clearWhiteboard: () => set(s => {
        s.whiteboardStrokes = []
        s.whiteboardShapes = []
      }),
      
      // ═════ MERMAID ACTIONS ═════
      setMermaidCode: (code) => set(s => { s.mermaidCode = code }),
      updateMermaidConfig: (config) => set(s => {
        Object.assign(s.mermaidConfig, config)
      }),
      setMermaidPreview: (svg) => set(s => { s.mermaidPreview = svg }),
      
      // ═════ MODULE ACTIONS — TASKS ═════
      addTask: (task) => set(s => {
        if (!task || !task.title) return
        s.tasks = [{
          ...task,
          id: uid("task"),
          createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
          updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
        }, ...s.tasks]
      }),
      
      updateTask: (id, patch) => set(s => {
        if (!id) return
        const idx = s.tasks.findIndex(t => t?.id === id)
        if (idx !== -1) {
          Object.assign(s.tasks[idx], {
            ...patch,
            updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
          })
        }
      }),
      
      deleteTask: (id) => set(s => {
        if (!id) return
        s.tasks = s.tasks.filter(t => t?.id !== id)
      }),
      
      moveTask: (id, status) => set(s => {
        if (!id) return
        const task = s.tasks.find(t => t?.id === id)
        if (task) {
          task.status = status
          task.updatedAt = new Date().toISOString()
        }
      }),
      
      // ═════ MODULE ACTIONS — PRESENTATIONS ═════
      addPresentation: (p) => {
        if (!p || !p.title) return ""
        const id = uid("pres")
        set(s => {
          s.presentations = [{
            ...p,
            id,
            createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
            updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
          }, ...s.presentations]
        })
        return id
      },
      
      updatePresentation: (id, patch) => set(s => {
        if (!id) return
        const idx = s.presentations.findIndex(p => p?.id === id)
        if (idx !== -1) {
          Object.assign(s.presentations[idx], {
            ...patch,
            updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
          })
        }
      }),
      
      deletePresentation: (id) => set(s => {
        if (!id) return
        s.presentations = s.presentations.filter(p => p?.id !== id)
      }),
      
      addSlide: (presentationId) => set(s => {
        if (!presentationId) return
        const pres = s.presentations.find(p => p?.id === presentationId)
        if (pres) {
          const newSlide: Slide = {
            id: uid("slide"),
            title: "New Slide",
            bg: "#08081f",
            elements: [{
              id: uid("elem"),
              kind: "text",
              x: 80, y: 120, w: 560, h: 80,
              content: "Click to edit",
              fontSize: 40,
              bold: true,
              color: "#f0f2f5"
            }],
            order: (pres.slides?.length || 0) + 1
          }
          pres.slides = [...(pres.slides || []), newSlide]
          pres.updatedAt = new Date().toISOString()
        }
      }),
      
      updateSlide: (presentationId, slideId, patch) => set(s => {
        if (!presentationId || !slideId) return
        const pres = s.presentations.find(p => p?.id === presentationId)
        if (!pres?.slides) return
        const slide = pres.slides.find(sl => sl?.id === slideId)
        if (slide) Object.assign(slide, patch)
      }),
      
      deleteSlide: (presentationId, slideId) => set(s => {
        if (!presentationId || !slideId) return
        const pres = s.presentations.find(p => p?.id === presentationId)
        if (pres?.slides) {
          pres.slides = pres.slides.filter(sl => sl?.id !== slideId)
          pres.updatedAt = new Date().toISOString()
        }
      }),
      
      // ═════ MODULE ACTIONS — CHARTS ═════
      addChart: (chart) => set(s => {
        if (!chart || !chart.title || !validateArray(chart.labels) || !validateArray(chart.datasets)) return
        s.charts = [{
          ...chart,
          id: uid("chart"),
          createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
          updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
        }, ...s.charts]
      }),
      
      updateChart: (id, patch) => set(s => {
        if (!id) return
        const idx = s.charts.findIndex(c => c?.id === id)
        if (idx !== -1) {
          Object.assign(s.charts[idx], {
            ...patch,
            updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
          })
        }
      }),
      
      deleteChart: (id) => set(s => {
        if (!id) return
        s.charts = s.charts.filter(c => c?.id !== id)
      }),
      
      // ═════ MODULE ACTIONS — COLLABORATION ═════
      addCollabDoc: (doc) => set(s => {
        if (!doc || !doc.title) return
        s.collabDocs = [{
          ...doc,
          id: uid("doc"),
          version: 1,
          createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
          updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
        }, ...s.collabDocs]
      }),
      
      updateCollabDoc: (id, patch) => set(s => {
        if (!id) return
        const idx = s.collabDocs.findIndex(d => d?.id === id)
        if (idx !== -1) {
          Object.assign(s.collabDocs[idx], {
            ...patch,
            updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
            version: (s.collabDocs[idx]?.version || 1) + 1
          })
        }
      }),
      
      deleteCollabDoc: (id) => set(s => {
        if (!id) return
        s.collabDocs = s.collabDocs.filter(d => d?.id !== id)
      }),
      
      // ═════ MODULE ACTIONS — PROPOSALS ═════
      addProposal: (p) => {
        if (!p || !p.title || !p.clientName) return ""
        const id = uid("prop")
        set(s => {
          s.proposals = [{
            ...p,
            id,
            status: "draft",
            createdAt: new Date().toISOString()
          }, ...s.proposals]
        })
        return id
      },
      
      updateProposal: (id, patch) => set(s => {
        if (!id) return
        const idx = s.proposals.findIndex(p => p?.id === id)
        if (idx !== -1) Object.assign(s.proposals[idx], patch)
      }),
      
      deleteProposal: (id) => set(s => {
        if (!id) return
        s.proposals = s.proposals.filter(p => p?.id !== id)
      }),
      
      addProposalLineItem: (proposalId, item) => set(s => {
        if (!proposalId || !item || !item.description) return
        const proposal = s.proposals.find(p => p?.id === proposalId)
        if (proposal?.lineItems) {
          proposal.lineItems.push({ ...item, id: uid("item") })
        }
      }),
      
      updateProposalLineItem: (proposalId, itemId, patch) => set(s => {
        if (!proposalId || !itemId) return
        const proposal = s.proposals.find(p => p?.id === proposalId)
        if (!proposal?.lineItems) return
        const item = proposal.lineItems.find(i => i?.id === itemId)
        if (item) Object.assign(item, patch)
      }),
      
      removeProposalLineItem: (proposalId, itemId) => set(s => {
        if (!proposalId || !itemId) return
        const proposal = s.proposals.find(p => p?.id === proposalId)
        if (proposal?.lineItems) {
          proposal.lineItems = proposal.lineItems.filter(i => i?.id !== itemId)
        }
      }),
      
      // ═════ AI ACTIONS ═════
      setAIProvider: (provider) => set(s => { s.aiProvider = provider }),
      
      addAIMessage: (conversationId, message) => set(s => {
        if (!s.aiConversations[conversationId]) {
          s.aiConversations[conversationId] = []
        }
        s.aiConversations[conversationId].push({
          ...message,
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        })
      }),
      
      clearAIConversation: (id) => set(s => {
        delete s.aiConversations[id]
      }),
      
      setAIContext: (context) => set(s => {
        Object.assign(s.currentAIContext, context)
      }),
      
      // ═════ UI ACTIONS ═════
      setTheme: (theme) => set(s => {
        s.theme = theme
        if (typeof document !== "undefined") {
          document.documentElement.setAttribute("data-theme", theme === "system" ? "dark" : theme)
        }
      }),
      
      addNotification: (n) => set(s => {
        s.notifications.unshift({
          ...n,
          id: uid("notif"),
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
          read: false
        })
        // Limit to 10 notifications
        if (s.notifications.length > 10) {
          s.notifications = s.notifications.slice(0, 10)
        }
      }),
      
      markNotificationRead: (id) => set(s => {
        const notif = s.notifications.find(n => n?.id === id)
        if (notif) notif.read = true
      }),
      
      removeNotification: (id) => set(s => {
        s.notifications = s.notifications.filter(n => n?.id !== id)
      }),
      
      updateSettings: (patch) => set(s => {
        Object.assign(s.settings, patch)
        // Sync theme if changed
        if (patch.theme) {
          s.theme = patch.theme
          if (typeof document !== "undefined") {
            document.documentElement.setAttribute("data-theme", patch.theme === "system" ? "dark" : patch.theme)
          }
        }
      })
    })),
    {
      name: "whisperx-ultimate",
      storage: createJSONStorage(() => {
        if (typeof window === "undefined") return undefined
        return localStorage
      }),
      partialize: (state) => ({
        // Persist only essential settings, not large canvas data
        theme: state.theme,
        settings: state.settings,
        workspace: {
          id: state.workspace.id,
          name: state.workspace.name,
          settings: state.workspace.settings
        },
        activeProjectId: state.activeProjectId
      })
    }
  )
)

{id:“b1”,label:“AI API Credits”,amount:2400,type:“expense”,date:“2025-04”,tag:“infra”},

],
docs:[
{id:“d1”,title:“NEXUS PRIME v27 Architecture”,content:”# Architecture\n\nv27.0-NEXUS-PRIME is the ultimate fusion of WhisperX v26-BLOOM, Zenith Omega, and Nexus Absolute.\n\n## Core Systems\n- Evolution Engine: AI-powered file analysis & code generation\n- Canvas Engine: Node graph with 56 types\n- Taxonomy Navigation: Feature→Workflow→Category→Module\n- Auth Tier System: 4-level access control”},
],
readinessItems:[
{id:“r1”,label:“Auth Gate”,             done:true,  sev:“ok”,      note:“4-tier login system”},

{id:“r10”,label:“Evolution Pipeline”,   done:true,  sev:“ok”,      note:“Full Vault→Forge→Archive”},

};

function reducer(state, action) {
switch(action.type){
case “SET_AUTH”:           return {…state,authTier:action.tier,authUser:action.user};
case “LOGOUT”:             return {…state,authTier:0,authUser:null,module:“overview”};
case “SET_MODULE”:         return {…state,module:action.id};
case “TOGGLE_SIDEBAR”:     return {…state,sidebarCollapsed:!state.sidebarCollapsed};
case “SET_SIDEBAR_MODE”:   return {…state,sidebarMode:action.mode};
case “TOGGLE_PALETTE”:     return {…state,palette:!state.palette};
case “TOGGLE_FEATURE”:     return {…state,expandedFeatures:state.expandedFeatures.includes(action.f)?state.expandedFeatures.filter(x=>x!==action.f):[…state.expandedFeatures,action.f]};
case “TOGGLE_WORKFLOW”:    return {…state,expandedWorkflows:state.expandedWorkflows.includes(action.id)?state.expandedWorkflows.filter(x=>x!==action.id):[…state.expandedWorkflows,action.id]};
case “TOGGLE_CATEGORY”:    return {…state,expandedCategories:state.expandedCategories.includes(action.k)?state.expandedCategories.filter(x=>x!==action.k):[…state.expandedCategories,action.k]};
case “VAULT_ADD”:          return {…state,vault:[action.file,…state.vault]};
case “VAULT_UPDATE”:       return {…state,vault:state.vault.map(f=>f.id===action.id?{…f,…action.patch}:f)};
case “VAULT_DELETE”:       return {…state,vault:state.vault.filter(f=>f.id!==action.id)};
case “EVO_ADD”:            return {…state,evoHistory:[action.entry,…state.evoHistory]};
case “EVO_DELETE”:         return {…state,evoHistory:state.evoHistory.filter(h=>h.id!==action.id)};
case “CANVAS_ADD_NODE”:    return {…state,canvasNodes:[…state.canvasNodes,action.node]};
case “CANVAS_UPDATE_NODE”: return {…state,canvasNodes:state.canvasNodes.map(n=>n.id===action.id?{…n,…action.patch}:n)};
case “CANVAS_DELETE_NODE”: return {…state,canvasNodes:state.canvasNodes.filter(n=>n.id!==action.id)};
case “CANVAS_ADD_EDGE”:    return {…state,canvasEdges:[…state.canvasEdges,action.edge]};
case “CANVAS_DELETE_EDGE”: return {…state,canvasEdges:state.canvasEdges.filter(e=>e.id!==action.id)};
case “CANVAS_SET_VIEW”:    return {…state,canvasPan:action.pan,canvasZoom:action.zoom};
case “TERMINAL_ADD”:       return {…state,terminalLines:[…state.terminalLines,action.line]};
case “TERMINAL_CLEAR”:     return {…state,terminalLines:[{text:“Terminal cleared.”,type:“dim”}]};
case “CONTACT_ADD”:        return {…state,contacts:[action.c,…state.contacts]};
case “CONTACT_DELETE”:     return {…state,contacts:state.contacts.filter(c=>c.id!==action.id)};
case “BUDGET_ADD”:         return {…state,budget:[action.item,…state.budget]};
case “BUDGET_DELETE”:      return {…state,budget:state.budget.filter(b=>b.id!==action.id)};
case “READINESS_TOGGLE”:   return {…state,readinessItems:state.readinessItems.map(r=>r.id===action.id?{…r,done:!r.done}:r)};
default: return state;
}
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  AI ENGINE — Claude Sonnet via Anthropic API
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
async function callAI(messages, system) {
const r = await fetch(“https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages”,{
method:“POST”,
headers:{“Content-Type”:“application/json”},
body:JSON.stringify({model:MODEL,max_tokens:1000,system,messages}),
});
const d = await r.json();
if(d.error) throw new Error(d.error.message);
return d.content.find(b=>b.type===“text”)?.text||””;
}

async function aiAnalyze(name,content,b64,kind){
const sys=`Logic extraction engine v27. Return ONLY valid JSON (no markdown fences):\n{"corePurpose":"one sharp sentence","dataType":"type label","abilities":["Label: description","Label: description","Label: description"]}`;
const uc = b64&&kind===“image”
? [{type:“image”,source:{type:“base64”,media_type:“image/jpeg”,data:b64}},{type:“text”,text:`Analyze image: ${name}`}]
: `Analyze file "${name}":\n\n${(content||"").slice(0,5000)}`;
const raw=(await callAI([{role:“user”,content:uc}],sys)).replace(/`json\n?|`\n?/g,””).trim();
return JSON.parse(raw);
}

async function aiEvolve(bp,ability,bpContent,mxName){
const sys=`Zenith Evolution Engine v27. Return ONLY valid JSON:\n{"newSystemName":"name","featureType":"SYNTHESIS|UPGRADE|FUSION","evolutionScore":98,"logicExplanation":"2 sentences","migrationNotes":"steps","breakingChanges":"none or list","evolvedContent":"COMPLETE CODE"}`;
const raw=(await callAI([{role:“user”,content:`BLUEPRINT:"${bp.name}"\nPURPOSE:"${bp.analysis?.corePurpose}"\nABILITY:"${ability}"\nMATRIX:"${mxName}"\nCONTENT:\n${(bpContent||"").slice(0,4000)}`}],sys)).replace(/`json\n?|`\n?/g,””).trim();
return JSON.parse(raw);
}

async function aiChat(messages){
const sys=`You are WhisperX NEXUS PRIME AI Terminal v27. You are a sharp, precise AI assistant embedded in a production OS. Be concise, technical, and helpful. Use code blocks for code.`;
return callAI(messages,sys);
}

// ─── LockSpec validation rules ───────────────────────────────────
function getErrors(vault,s1,s2,ability){
const done=vault.filter(f=>f.status===“done”);
if(vault.length===0)return[{code:“I001”,sev:“info”,msg:“Vault empty”,fix:“Import files first”}];
const e=[];
if(done.length<2)e.push({code:“I002”,sev:“info”,msg:“Need ≥2 analyzed files”,fix:“Import & analyze more”});
if(!s1)e.push({code:“E001”,sev:“error”,msg:“No Blueprint selected”,fix:“Select Slot 01”});
if(!s2)e.push({code:“E002”,sev:“error”,msg:“No Matrix selected”,fix:“Select Slot 02”});
if(s1&&s2&&s1===s2)e.push({code:“W001”,sev:“warning”,msg:“Blueprint = Matrix”,fix:“Select different files”});
if(s1&&s2&&s1!==s2&&!ability)e.push({code:“E003”,sev:“error”,msg:“No Ability selected”,fix:“Choose an ability”});
return e;
}

// ─── Reducer (v27) ──────────────────────────────────────────────
function reducer(state, action) {
switch(action.type){
case “SET_AUTH”:           return {…state,authTier:action.tier,authUser:action.user};
case “LOGOUT”:             return {…state,authTier:0,authUser:null,module:“overview”};
case “SET_MODULE”:         return {…state,module:action.id};
case “TOGGLE_SIDEBAR”:     return {…state,sidebarCollapsed:!state.sidebarCollapsed};
case “SET_SIDEBAR_MODE”:   return {…state,sidebarMode:action.mode};
case “TOGGLE_PALETTE”:     return {…state,palette:!state.palette};
case “TOGGLE_FEATURE”:     return {…state,expandedFeatures:state.expandedFeatures.includes(action.f)?state.expandedFeatures.filter(x=>x!==action.f):[…state.expandedFeatures,action.f]};
case “TOGGLE_WORKFLOW”:    return {…state,expandedWorkflows:state.expandedWorkflows.includes(action.id)?state.expandedWorkflows.filter(x=>x!==action.id):[…state.expandedWorkflows,action.id]};
case “TOGGLE_CATEGORY”:    return {…state,expandedCategories:state.expandedCategories.includes(action.k)?state.expandedCategories.filter(x=>x!==action.k):[…state.expandedCategories,action.k]};
case “VAULT_ADD”:          return {…state,vault:[action.file,…state.vault]};
case “VAULT_UPDATE”:       return {…state,vault:state.vault.map(f=>f.id===action.id?{…f,…action.patch}:f)};
case “VAULT_DELETE”:       return {…state,vault:state.vault.filter(f=>f.id!==action.id)};
case “EVO_ADD”:            return {…state,evoHistory:[action.entry,…state.evoHistory]};
case “EVO_DELETE”:         return {…state,evoHistory:state.evoHistory.filter(h=>h.id!==action.id)};
case “CANVAS_ADD_NODE”:    return {…state,canvasNodes:[…state.canvasNodes,action.node]};
case “CANVAS_UPDATE_NODE”: return {…state,canvasNodes:state.canvasNodes.map(n=>n.id===action.id?{…n,…action.patch}:n)};
case “CANVAS_DELETE_NODE”: return {…state,canvasNodes:state.canvasNodes.filter(n=>n.id!==action.id)};
case “CANVAS_ADD_EDGE”:    return {…state,canvasEdges:[…state.canvasEdges,action.edge]};

case “BUDGET_ADD”:         return {…state,budget:[action.item,…state.budget]};
case “BUDGET_DELETE”:      return {…state,budget:state.budget.filter(b=>b.id!==action.id)};
case “READINESS_TOGGLE”:   return {…state,readinessItems:state.readinessItems.map(r=>r.id===action.id?{…r,done:!r.done}:r)};
default: return state;
}
}

//  FILE INGEST
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// ─── React context ───────────────────────────────────────────────
import { createContext, useContext, useReducer, type ReactNode } from "react";

type State = typeof initState;
type Action = { type: string; [key: string]: unknown };

const StoreCtx = createContext<{
  state: State;
  dispatch: React.Dispatch<Action>;
} | null>(null);

export function StoreProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
  const [state, dispatch] = useReducer(reducer as React.Reducer<State, Action>, initState);
  return <StoreCtx.Provider value={{ state, dispatch }}>{children}</StoreCtx.Provider>;
}

export function useStore() {
  const ctx = useContext(StoreCtx);
  if (!ctx) throw new Error("useStore must be used inside StoreProvider");
  return ctx;
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  WHISPERX NEXUS OMEGA — Type Definitions
//  Merged: MergeV types + v27 state types + Vision pipeline types
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// ─── Canvas ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
export type NodeShape = "rect" | "hex" | "diamond" | "circle" | "pill" | "octagon";
export type NodeType = "process" | "ai-core" | "evolve" | "llm" | "vault" | "decision" |
  "start" | "end" | "loop" | "gate" | "io" | "db" | "api" | "user" | "system" | "cloud";

export interface CanvasNode {
  id: string; x: number; y: number; w: number; h: number;
  label: string; type: NodeType; color: string; shape: NodeShape; z: number;
  data?: Record<string, unknown>;
}

export interface CanvasEdge {
  id: string; from: string; to: string; label?: string; color?: string;
}

// ─── Vault ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
export type FileKind = "text" | "image" | "pdf" | "binary";
export type FileStatus = "pending" | "analyzing" | "done" | "error";

export interface VaultAnalysis {
  corePurpose: string; dataType: string;
  abilities: string[]; keyEntities?: string[];
}

// ─── Forge / Evolution ────────────────────────────────────────
export type FeatureType = "SYNTHESIS" | "ENHANCEMENT" | "FUSION" | "UPGRADE";

export interface EvolutionResult {
  newSystemName: string; featureType: FeatureType; evolutionScore: number;
  logicExplanation: string; evolvedContent: string;
  migrationNotes: string; breakingChanges: string;
  blueprintName: string; matrixName: string; appliedAbility: string;
  timestamp: string;
}

// ─── Vision Pipeline ──────────────────────────────────────────
export type VisionStageStatus = "idle" | "running" | "done" | "error";
export type SourceType = "lockspec" | "feature_spec" | "implementation_plan" | "vision_import";

export interface VisionStageState {
  id: string; status: VisionStageStatus; message: string; tokens: number;
}

export interface VisionImportResult {
  sourceName: string; detectedType: SourceType; confidence: number;
  lockspecText: string; signals: StructuralSignals;
  stages: VisionStageState[]; totalTokens: number;
}

export interface StructuralSignals {
  headings: string[]; bullets: string[]; codeBlocks: string[];
  filePaths: string[]; routeHints: string[]; menuHints: string[];
  configPairs: Array<{ key: string; value: string }>;
  destructiveHints: string[]; commands: string[];
}

// ─── UI ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
export type ToastType = "ok" | "error" | "warning" | "info";
export interface ToastMessage { msg: string; type: ToastType }

// ─── Store / Access Tiers ─────────────────────────────────────
export type AccessTier = 0 | 1 | 2 | 3;
export type ModuleId = "overview" | "workspace" | "forge" | "vault" | "archive" |
  "ai" | "terminal" | "summary" | "history" | "readiness" | "docs" | "slides" |
  "reader" | "topology" | "contacts" | "budget" | "settings" | "vision";

Invoke-Step "Verify Node.js" {
  if (-not (Get-Command node -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue)) { throw "Node.js not found — https://nodejs.org" }
  $v = node --version; Write-Host "    Node $v" -ForegroundColor DarkGray
}

Invoke-Step "Install dependencies" {
  npm install --legacy-peer-deps 2>&1 | Select-Object -Last 8
}

Write-Host ""
Write-Host "  ╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗" -ForegroundColor Green
Write-Host "  ║  Installation Complete!                                       ║" -ForegroundColor Green
Write-Host "  ╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝" -ForegroundColor Green
Write-Host ""
Write-Host "  Next Steps:" -ForegroundColor Yellow
Write-Host "  1. Add GEMINI_API_KEY to .env.local" -ForegroundColor DarkGray
Write-Host "  2. npm run dev" -ForegroundColor DarkGray
Write-Host "  3. http://localhost:3000" -ForegroundColor Cyan
Write-Host ""

$launch = Read-Host "  Launch dev server now? (y/N)"
if ($launch -eq "y" -or $launch -eq "Y") {
  $k = Read-Host "  GEMINI_API_KEY (or Enter to set later)"
  if ($k) { "GEMINI_API_KEY=$k`nAPP_URL=http://localhost:3000" | Set-Content .env.local -Encoding UTF8 }
  Write-Host "  Starting..." -ForegroundColor Cyan
  npm run dev
}
